{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-1-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-3}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}}\(\Sigma\)-recursivas

\hypertarget{el-paradigma-imperativo-de-neumann-el-lenguaje-mathcalssigma}{%
\subsection[{4.3} El paradigma imperativo de Neumann: El lenguaje
\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3} El paradigma imperativo
de Neumann: El lenguaje
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-2-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-4}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-5}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}{4.3 El paradigma imperativo de Neumann: El lenguaje SΣ\textbackslash mathcal\{S\}\^{}\{\textbackslash Sigma\}\textbackslash mathcal\{S\}\^{}\{\textbackslash Sigma\}}}\label{el-paradigma-imperativo-de-neumann-el-lenguaje-mathcalssigma}}

En esta sección daremos una modelización matemática del concepto de
función
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3.1-funciones-sigma-efectivamente-computables.html\#definicion\%20de\%20funcion\%20sigma-efectivamente\%20computable}{{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-3-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable utilizando un lenguaje de programación teórico el cual
depende del alfabeto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-4-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\).
Lo llamaremos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-5-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-21}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-22}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-23}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-24}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-25}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-26}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-27}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
a dicho lenguaje. Dado que fue el matemático Von Neumann quien
contribuyo al desarrollo de la primera computadora de propósito general
(es decir a la cual se le pueden hacer correr programas tal como a las
computadoras actuales), nos referiremos a este paradigma de
computabilidad efectiva como el \emph{paradigma de Von Neumann}. También
lo llamaremos algunas veces el \emph{paradigma imperativo}.

\hypertarget{sintaxis-de-mathcalssigma}{%
\subsubsection[{4.3.1} Sintaxis de
\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.1}
\protect\hypertarget{SintaxisDeSsigma}{}{}Sintaxis de
{{}\protect\hypertarget\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}
Dec(0) & =\varepsilon\\
Dec(n+1) & =Sig(Dec(n))
\end{aligned}\] Nótese que para
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-14-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-333}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-334}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-335}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-336}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-337}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-338}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-339}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(n \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(n\in\mathbf{N}\),
la palabra
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-15-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-340}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-341}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-342}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-343}{}{{e}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-344}{}{{c}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-345}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-346}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-347}{}{{)}}}}{\(Dec(n)\)}}}\(Dec(n)\)
es la notación usual decimal de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-16-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-348}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-349}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-350}{}{{n}}}}{\(n\)}}}\(n\).
Para hacer mas ágil la notación escribiremos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-17-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-351}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-352}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-353}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-354}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-355}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-357}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-356}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\(\overline{n}\)}}}\(\bar{n}\)
en lugar de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-18-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-358}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-359}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-360}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-361}{}{{e}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-362}{}{{c}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-363}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-364}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-365}{}{{)}}}}{\(Dec(n)\)}}}\(Dec(n)\).
Nótese que, en virtud de esta convención notacional se tiene que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-19-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-366}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-367}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-368}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-369}{}{{e}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-370}{}{{c}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-371}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-372}{}{{λ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-373}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-374}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-375}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-376}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-377}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-379}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-378}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-380}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(Dec = \lambda n\lbrack\overline{n}\rbrack\)}}}\(Dec=\lambda n[\bar{n}]\).
La sintaxis de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-20-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-381}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-382}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-383}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-384}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-385}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-386}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-387}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-388}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-389}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
será dada utilizando solo símbolos del alfabeto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-21-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-390}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-391}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-392}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-393}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-394}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-395}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-396}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-397}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-398}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma \cup \Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma\cup\Sigma_{p}\),
donde
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-22-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-399}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-400}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-401}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-402}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-403}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-404}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-405}{}{{p}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-406}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-407}{}{{N}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-408}{}{{u}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-409}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-410}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-411}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-412}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-413}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-414}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-415}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-416}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-417}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-418}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-419}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-421}{}{{˙}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-420}{}{{−}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-422}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-423}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-424}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-425}{}{{≠}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-426}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-427}{}{{,}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-428}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-429}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-430}{}{{↷}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-431}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-432}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-433}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-434}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-435}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-436}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-437}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-438}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-439}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-440}{}{{K}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-441}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-442}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-443}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-444}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-445}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-446}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-447}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-448}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-449}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-450}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-451}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-452}{}{{I}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-453}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-454}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-455}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-456}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-457}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-458}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-459}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-460}{}{{G}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-461}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-462}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-463}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-464}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-465}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-466}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-467}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-468}{}{{T}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-469}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-470}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-471}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-472}{}{{B}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-473}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-474}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-475}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-476}{}{{E}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-477}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-478}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-479}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-480}{}{{S}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-481}{}{{\}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-482}{}{{.}}}}{\[\Sigma_{p} = Num \cup \left\{ \leftarrow, + ,\overset{˙}{-},., \neq ,^{\curvearrowright},\varepsilon,N,K,P,L,I,F,G,O,T,B,E,S \right\}.\]}}}}\[\Sigma_{p}=Num\cup\left\{
\leftarrow,+,\dot{-},.,\neq,^{\curvearrowright},\varepsilon,\mathrm{N},\mathrm{K},\mathrm{P},\mathrm{L},\mathrm{I},\mathrm{F},\mathrm{G},\mathrm{O},\mathrm{T},\mathrm{B},\mathrm{E},\mathrm{S}\right\}
.\] Cabe aclarar que la palabra de longitud
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-23-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-483}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-484}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-485}{}{{0}}}}{\(0\)}}}\(0\)
no es un elemento de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-24-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-486}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-487}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-488}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-489}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-490}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-491}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-492}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma_{p}\)
sino que la letra griega
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-25-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-493}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-494}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-495}{}{{ε}}}}{\(\varepsilon\)}}}\(\varepsilon\)
que usualmente denota esta palabra, lo es. También nótese que en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-26-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-496}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-497}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-498}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-499}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-500}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-501}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-502}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma_{p}\)
hay símbolos que a veces representan operaciones como por ejemplo
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-27-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-503}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-504}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-505}{}{{+}}}}{\(+\)}}}\(+\)
,
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-28-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-506}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-507}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-508}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-509}{}{{}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-510}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-511}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-512}{}{{↷}}}}}}}}{\(^{\curvearrowright}\)}}}\(^{\curvearrowright}\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-29-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-513}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-514}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-515}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-516}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-517}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-519}{}{{˙}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-518}{}{{−}}}}}}}}}{\(\overset{˙}{-}\)}}}\(\dot{-}\),
pero debería quedar claro que en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-30-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-520}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-521}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-522}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-523}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-524}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-525}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-526}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma_{p}\)
están los símbolos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-31-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-527}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-528}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-529}{}\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}
\text{INSTRUCCION} &
:\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\leftarrow\mathrm{P}\bar{k}.a\\
\text{INTERPRETACION} & :\begin{array}[t]{l}
\text{Modificar el contenido de }\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\text{ agregandole}\\
\text{el simbolo }a\text{ a la derecha}
\end{array}\\
\text{INSTRUCCION} &
:\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;a\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{m}\\
\text{INTERPRETACION} & :\begin{array}[t]{l}
\text{Si el contenido de }\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\text{ comiensa con
}a,\text{ejecute}\\
\text{la primer instruccion con label }\mathrm{L}\bar{m}\text{; en
caso}\\
\text{contrario ejecute la siguiente instruccion}
\end{array}
\end{aligned}\]

\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20programa}{}{}Un \emph{programa
de}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-82-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1538}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1539}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1540}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1541}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1542}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1543}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1544}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1545}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1546}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
es una palabra de la forma
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-83-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1547}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1548}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1549}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1550}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1551}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1552}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1553}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1554}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1555}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1556}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1557}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1558}{}{{2}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1559}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1560}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1561}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1562}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1563}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1564}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1565}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1566}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\[I_{1}I_{2}...I_{n}\]}}}}\[I_{1}I_{2}...I_{n}\]
donde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-84-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1567}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1568}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1569}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1570}{}{{≥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1571}{}{{1}}}}{\(n \geq 1\)}}}\(n\geq1\),
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-85-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1572}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1573}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1574}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1575}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1576}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1577}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1578}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1579}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1580}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1581}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1582}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1583}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1584}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1585}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1586}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1587}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1588}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1589}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1590}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1591}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1592}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1593}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1594}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1595}{}{{s}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1596}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1597}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1598}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1},...,I_{n} \in {Ins}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(I_{1},...,I_{n}\in\mathrm{Ins}^{\Sigma}\)
y además se cumple la siguiente propiedad, llamada \emph{la ley de los
GOTO},

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  (G) Para cada
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-86-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1599}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1600}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1601}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1602}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1603}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1604}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1605}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1606}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1607}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1608}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1609}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1610}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1611}{}{{\}}}}}{\(i \in \{ 1,...,n\}\)}}}\(i\in\{1,...,n\}\),
  si
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-87-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1612}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1613}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1614}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1615}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1616}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1617}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1618}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1619}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1620}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1621}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1622}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1623}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1625}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1624}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\({GOTOL}\overline{m}\)}}}\(\mathrm{GOTOL}\bar{m}\)
  es un tramo final de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-88-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1626}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1627}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1628}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1629}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1630}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1631}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1632}{}{{i}}}}}}}}{\(I_{i}\)}}}\(I_{i}\),
  entonces existe
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-89-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1633}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1634}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1635}{}{{j}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1636}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1637}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1638}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1639}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1640}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1641}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1642}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1643}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1644}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1645}{}{{\}}}}}{\(j \in \{ 1,...,n\}\)}}}\(j\in\{1,...,n\}\)
  tal que
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-90-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1646}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1647}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1648}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1649}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1650}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1651}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1652}{}{{j}}}}}}}}{\(I_{j}\)}}}\(I_{j}\)
  tiene label
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-91-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1653}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1654}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1655}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1656}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1657}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1658}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1659}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1660}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1662}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1661}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\(L\overline{m}\)}}}\(\mathrm{L}\bar{m}\)
\end{enumerate}

Usaremos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-92-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1663}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1664}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1665}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1666}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1667}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1668}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1669}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1670}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1671}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1672}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1673}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\({Pro}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\)
para denotar el conjunto de todos los programas de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-93-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1674}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1675}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1676}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1677}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1678}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1679}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1680}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1681}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1682}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\).
Como es usual cuando escribamos un programa lo haremos linea por linea,
con la finalidad de que sea mas legible. Por ejemplo, escribiremos

{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1730}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1731}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1732}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1733}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1734}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1735}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1736}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1737}{}{{F}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1738}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1739}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1740}{}{{12}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1741}{}{{≠}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1742}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1743}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1744}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1745}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1746}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1747}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1748}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1749}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1750}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1751}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1752}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1753}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1754}{}{{2}}{}}}}}}}}{\[\begin{matrix}
{L2} & {N12\leftarrow N12\overset{˙}{-}1} \\
 & {P1\leftarrow\ ^{\curvearrowright}P1} \\
 & {{IF\; N}12 \neq 0\;{GOTO}\; L2}
\end{matrix}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{ll}
\mathrm{L}2 & \mathrm{N}12\leftarrow\mathrm{N}12\dot{-}1\\
& \mathrm{P}1\leftarrow\text{ }^{\curvearrowright}\mathrm{P}1\\

\neq 0{GOTOL}2\]}}}}\[\mathrm{L}2\mathrm{N}12\mathrm{\leftarrow}\text{N}12\mathrm{\dot{-}}1\mathrm{P}1\mathrm{\leftarrow}^{\curvearrowright}\mathrm{P}1\mathrm{IFN}12\mathrm{\neq}0\mathrm{GOTOL}2\]
Un importante resultado es el siguiente lema que garantiza que los
programas pueden ser parseados en forma única como concatenación de
instrucciones.

\textbf{4.41}. \emph{Se tiene que:}

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  \emph{(a) Si
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-96-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1811}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1812}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1813}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1814}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1815}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1816}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1817}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1818}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1819}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1820}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1821}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1822}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1823}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1824}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1825}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1826}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1827}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1828}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1829}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1830}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1831}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1832}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1833}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1834}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1835}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1836}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1837}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1838}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1839}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1}...I_{n} = J_{1}...J_{m}\)}}}}\(I_{1}...I_{n}=J_{1}...J_{m}\),
  con
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-97-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1840}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1841}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1842}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1843}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1844}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1845}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1846}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1847}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1848}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1849}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1850}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1851}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1852}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1853}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1854}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1855}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1856}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1857}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1858}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1859}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1860}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1861}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1862}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1863}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1864}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1865}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1866}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1867}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1868}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1869}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1870}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1871}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1872}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1873}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1874}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1875}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1876}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1877}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1878}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1879}{}{{s}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1880}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1881}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1882}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1},...,I_{n},J_{1},...,J_{m} \in {Ins}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(I_{1},...,I_{n},J_{1},...,J_{m}\in\mathrm{Ins}^{\Sigma}\),
  entonces
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-98-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1883}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1884}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1885}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1886}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1887}{}{{m}}}}{\(n = m\)}}}\(n=m\)
  y
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-99-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1888}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1889}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1890}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1891}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1892}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1893}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1894}{}{{j}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1895}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1896}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1897}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1898}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1899}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1900}{}{{j}}}}}}}}{\(I_{j} = J_{j}\)}}}\(I_{j}=J_{j}\)
  para cada
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-100-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1901}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1902}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1903}{}{{j}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1904}{}{{≥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1905}{}{{1}}}}{\(j \geq 1\)}}}\(j\geq1\).
\item
  \emph{(b) Si
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-101-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1906}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1907}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1908}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1909}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1910}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1911}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1912}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1913}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1914}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1915}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1916}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1917}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1918}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1919}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1920}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} \in {Pro}^{\Sigma}\)}}}}\(\mathcal{P}\in\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\),
  entonces existe una única sucesión de instrucciones
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-102-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1921}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1922}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1923}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1924}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1925}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1926}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1927}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1928}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1929}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1930}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1931}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1932}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1933}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1934}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1935}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1936}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1937}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1},...,I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{1},...,I_{n}\)
  tal que
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-103-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1938}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1939}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1940}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1941}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1942}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1943}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1944}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1945}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1946}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1947}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1948}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1949}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1950}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1951}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1952}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1953}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1954}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1955}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1956}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} = I_{1}...I_{n}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}=I_{1}...I_{n}\)
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{Proof.} (a) Supongamos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-104-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1957}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1958}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1959}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1960}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1961}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1962}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1963}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1964}{}{{≠}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1965}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1966}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1967}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1968}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1969}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n} \neq J_{m}\)}}}\(I_{n}\neq J_{m}\).
Ya que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-105-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1970}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1971}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1972}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1973}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1974}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1975}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1976}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1977}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1978}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1979}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1980}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1981}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1982}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1983}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1984}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1985}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1986}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1987}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1988}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1989}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1990}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1991}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1992}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1993}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1994}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1995}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1996}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1997}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1998}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1}...I_{n} = J_{1}...J_{m}\)}}}\(I_{1}...I_{n}=J_{1}...J_{m}\)
tenemos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-106-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-1999}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2000}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2001}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2002}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2003}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2004}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2005}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{n}\)
es un tramo final propio de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-107-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2006}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2007}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2008}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2009}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2010}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2011}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2012}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m}\)}}}\(J_{m}\)
o
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-108-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2013}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2014}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2015}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2016}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2017}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2018}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2019}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m}\)}}}\(J_{m}\)
es un tramo final propio de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-109-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2020}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2021}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2022}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2023}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2024}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2025}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2026}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2027}{}{{.}}}}{\(I_{n}.\)}}}\(I_{n}.\)
Supongamos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-110-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2028}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2029}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2030}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2031}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2032}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2033}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2034}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{n}\)
es un tramo final propio de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-111-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2035}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2036}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2037}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2038}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2039}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2040}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2041}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2042}{}{{.}}}}{\(J_{m}.\)}}}\(J_{m}.\)
Notar que entonces
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-112-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2043}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2044}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2045}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2046}{}{{\textgreater{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2047}{}{{1}}}}{\(n > 1\)}}}\(n>1\).
Es fácil ver que entonces ya sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-113-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2048}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2049}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2050}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2051}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2052}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2053}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2054}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2055}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2056}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2057}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2058}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2059}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2060}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2061}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2063}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2062}{}{{u}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2064}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2065}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2066}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2067}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2068}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m} = L\overline{u}I_{n}\)}}}\(J_{m}=\mathrm{L}\bar{u}I_{n}\)
para algún
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-114-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2069}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2070}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2071}{}{{u}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2072}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2073}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2074}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2075}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(u \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(u\in\mathbf{N}\),
o
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-115-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2076}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2077}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2078}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2079}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2080}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2081}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2082}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{n}\)
es de la forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-116-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2083}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2084}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2085}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2086}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2087}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2088}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2089}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2090}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2091}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2092}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2093}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2094}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2095}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2096}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2097}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2099}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2098}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\({GOTO}\; L\overline{n}\)}}}\(\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{n}\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-117-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2100}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2101}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2102}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2103}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2104}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2105}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2106}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m}\)}}}\(J_{m}\)
es de la forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-118-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2107}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2108}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2109}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2110}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2111}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2112}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2113}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2114}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2115}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2116}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2117}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2118}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2119}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2120}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2122}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2121}{}{{k}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2123}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2124}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2125}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2126}{}{{B}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2127}{}{{E}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2128}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2129}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2130}{}{{N}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2131}{}{{S}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2132}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2133}{}{{a}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2134}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2135}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2136}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2137}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2138}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2139}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2140}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2141}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2142}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2143}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2144}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2145}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2146}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2147}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2149}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2148}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\(\alpha{IF}\; P\overline{k}\;{BEGINS}\; a\;{GOTO}\; L\overline{n}\)}}}\(\alpha\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;a\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{n}\)
con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-119-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2150}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2151}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2152}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2153}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2154}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2155}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2156}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2157}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2158}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2159}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2160}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2162}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2161}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2163}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2164}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2165}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2166}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2167}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2168}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2169}{}{{\}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2170}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2171}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2172}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2173}{}{{\}}}}}{\(\alpha \in \{ L\overline{n}:n \in \mathbf{N}\} \cup \{\varepsilon\}\)}}}\(\alpha\in\{\mathrm{L}\bar{n}:n\in\mathbf{N}\}\cup\{\varepsilon\}\).
El segundo caso no puede darse porque entonces el anteúltimo símbolo de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-120-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2174}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2175}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2176}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2177}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2178}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2179}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2180}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2181}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2182}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n - 1}\)}}}\(I_{n-1}\)
debería ser
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-121-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2183}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2184}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2185}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2186}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2187}{}{{S}}}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(\mathrm{S}\)
lo cual no sucede para ninguna instrucción. O sea que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-122-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2188}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2189}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2190}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2191}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2192}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2193}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2194}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2195}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2196}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2197}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2198}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2199}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2200}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2201}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2203}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2202}{}{{u}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2204}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2205}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2206}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2207}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2208}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m} = L\overline{u}I_{n}\)}}}\(J_{m}=\mathrm{L}\bar{u}I_{n}\)
para algún
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-123-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2209}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2210}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2211}{}{{u}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2212}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2213}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2214}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2215}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(u \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(u\in\mathbf{N}\),
por lo cual tenemos que
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-124-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2216}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2217}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2218}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2219}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2220}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2221}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2222}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2223}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2224}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2225}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2226}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2227}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2228}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2229}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2230}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2231}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2232}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2233}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2234}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2235}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2236}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2237}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2238}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2239}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2240}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2241}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2242}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2243}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2244}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2245}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2246}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2247}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2248}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2249}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2250}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2251}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2252}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2254}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2253}{}{{u}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2255}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2256}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2257}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2258}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2259}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\[I_{1}...I_{n} = J_{1}...J_{m - 1}L\overline{u}I_{n}\]}}}}\[I_{1}...I_{n}=J_{1}...J_{m-1}\mathrm{L}\bar{u}I_{n}\]
Pero esto nos dice que

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  ({*})
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-125-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2260}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2261}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2262}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2263}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2264}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2265}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2266}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2267}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2268}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2269}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2270}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2271}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2272}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2273}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2274}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2275}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2276}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2277}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2278}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2279}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2280}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2281}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2282}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2283}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2284}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2285}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2286}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2287}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2288}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2289}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2290}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2291}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2292}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2293}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2294}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2295}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2296}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2297}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2298}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2300}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2299}{}{{u}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2301}{}{{.}}}}{\(I_{1}...I_{n - 1} = J_{1}...J_{m - 1}L\overline{u}.\)}}}\(I_{1}...I_{n-1}=J_{1}...J_{m-1}\mathrm{L}\bar{u}.\)
\end{enumerate}

Es fácil deducir entonces que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-126-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2302}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2303}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2304}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2305}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2306}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2307}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2308}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2309}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2311}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2310}{}{{u}}}}}}}}}{\(L\overline{u}\)}}}\(\mathrm{L}\bar{u}\)
es tramo final de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-127-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2312}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2313}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2314}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2315}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2316}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2317}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2318}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2319}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2320}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n - 1}\)}}}\(I_{n-1}\)
y por lo tanto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-128-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2321}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2323}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2324}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2325}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2326}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2327}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2328}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2329}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2330}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2331}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2332}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2333}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2334}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2335}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2337}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2336}{}{{u}}}}}}}}}{\({GOTO}\; L\overline{u}\)}}}\(\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{u}\)
es tramo final de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-129-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2338}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2339}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2340}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2341}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2342}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2343}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2344}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2345}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2346}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n - 1}\)}}}\(I_{n-1}\).
Pero entonces por ({*}), tenemos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-130-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2347}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2348}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2349}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2350}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2351}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2352}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2353}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2354}{}{{O}}}}}}{\(GOTO\)}}}\(\mathrm{GOTO}\)
es tramo final de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-131-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2355}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2356}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2357}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2358}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2359}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2360}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2361}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2362}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2363}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2364}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2365}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2366}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2367}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2368}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2369}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2370}{}{{−}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2371}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(J_{1}...J_{m - 1}\)}}}\(J_{1}...J_{m-1}\),
lo cual es imposible. Hemos llegado a una contradicción lo cual nos dice
que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-132-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2372}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2373}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2374}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2375}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2376}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2377}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2378}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{n}\)
no es un tramo final propio de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-133-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2379}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2380}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2381}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2382}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2383}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2384}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2385}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2386}{}{{.}}}}{\(J_{m}.\)}}}\(J_{m}.\)
Por simetría tenemos también que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-134-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2387}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2388}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2389}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2390}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2391}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2392}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2393}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(J_{m}\)}}}\(J_{m}\)
no es un tramo final propio de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-135-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2394}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2395}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2396}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2397}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2398}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2399}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2400}{}{{n}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n}\)}}}\(I_{n}\),
arribando a un absurdo. O sea que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-136-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2401}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2402}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2403}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2404}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2405}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2406}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2407}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2408}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2409}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2410}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2411}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2412}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2413}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n} = J_{m}\)}}}\(I_{n}=J_{m}\).
Usando un razonamiento inductivo obtenemos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-137-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2414}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2415}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2416}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2417}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2418}{}{{m}}}}{\(n = m\)}}}\(n=m\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-138-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2419}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2420}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2421}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2422}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2423}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2424}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2425}{}{{j}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2426}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2427}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2428}{}{{J}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2429}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2430}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2431}{}{{j}}}}}}}}{\(I_{j} = J_{j}\)}}}\(I_{j}=J_{j}\)
para cada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-139-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2432}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2433}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2434}{}{{j}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2435}{}{{≥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2436}{}{{1}}}}{\(j \geq 1\)}}}\(j\geq1\).

(b) Es consecuencia directa de (a). ~

(b) del lema anterior nos dice que dado un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-140-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2437}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2438}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2439}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2440}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2441}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\),
tenemos unívocamente determinados

y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-142-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2454}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2455}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2456}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2457}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2461}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2462}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2463}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2464}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2465}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2458}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2459}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2460}{}{{1}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2466}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2467}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2468}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2469}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2470}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2471}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2472}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2481}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2482}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2483}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2484}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2485}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2473}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2474}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2475}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2476}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2477}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2478}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2479}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2480}{}{{)}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2486}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2487}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2488}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2489}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2490}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2491}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2492}{}{{s}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2493}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2494}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2495}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(I_{1}^{\mathcal{P}},...,I_{n(\mathcal{P})}^{\mathcal{P}} \in {Ins}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(I_{1}^{\mathcal{P}},...,I_{n(\mathcal{P})}^{\mathcal{P}}\in\mathrm{Ins}^{\Sigma}\)
tales que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-143-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2496}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2497}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2498}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2499}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2500}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2501}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2502}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2503}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2507}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2508}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2509}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2510}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2511}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2504}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2505}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2506}{}{{1}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2512}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2513}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2514}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2515}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2516}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2525}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2526}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2527}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2528}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2529}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2517}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2518}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2519}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2520}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2521}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2522}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2523}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2524}{}{{)}}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} = I_{1}^{\mathcal{P}}...I_{n(\mathcal{P})}^{\mathcal{P}}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}=I_{1}^{\mathcal{P}}...I_{n(\mathcal{P})}^{\mathcal{P}}\).
Definamos también
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-144-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2530}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2531}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2532}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2533}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2537}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2538}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2539}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2540}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2541}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2534}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2535}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2536}{}{{i}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2542}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2543}{}{{ε}}}}{\[I_{i}^{\mathcal{P}} = \varepsilon\]}}}}\[I_{i}^{\mathcal{P}}=\varepsilon\]
cuando
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-145-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2544}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2545}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2546}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2547}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2548}{}{{0}}}}{\(i = 0\)}}}\(i=0\)
o
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-146-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2549}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2550}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2551}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2552}{}{{\textgreater{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2553}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2554}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2555}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2556}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2557}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2558}{}{{)}}}}{\(i > n(\mathcal{P})\)}}}\(i>n(\mathcal{P})\).
Nótese que las expresiones
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-147-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2559}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2560}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2561}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2562}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2563}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2564}{}{{)}}}}{\(n(\alpha)\)}}}\(n(\alpha)\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-148-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2565}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2566}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2567}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2568}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2572}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2573}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2574}{}{{α}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2569}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2570}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2571}{}{{i}}}}}}}}}{\(I_{i}^{\alpha}\)}}}\(I_{i}^{\alpha}\)
están definidas solo cuando
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-149-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2575}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2576}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2577}{}{{α}}}}{\(\alpha\)}}}\(\alpha\)
es un programa (y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-150-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2578}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2579}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2580}{}{{i}}}}{\(i\)}}}\(i\)
es un elemento de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-151-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2581}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2582}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2583}{}{{ω}}}}{\(\omega\)}}}\(\omega\)),
es decir, cierta palabra del alfabeto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-152-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2584}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2585}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2586}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2587}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2588}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2589}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2590}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2591}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2592}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma \cup \Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma\cup\Sigma_{p}\).
O sea que cuando usemos notación lambda que involucre dichas
expresiones, el alfabeto respecto del cual usaremos dicha notación será
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-153-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2593}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2594}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2595}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2596}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2597}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2598}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2599}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2600}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2601}{}{{p}}}}}}}}{\(\Sigma \cup \Sigma_{p}\)}}}\(\Sigma\cup\Sigma_{p}\).
Esto nos dice entonces que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-154-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2602}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2603}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2604}{}{{λ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2605}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2606}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2607}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2608}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2609}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2610}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2611}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(\lambda\alpha\lbrack n(\alpha)\rbrack\)}}}\(\lambda\alpha[n(\alpha)]\)
tiene dominio igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-155-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2612}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2613}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2614}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2615}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2616}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2617}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2618}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2619}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2620}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2621}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2622}{}{{Σ}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2623}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2624}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2625}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2626}{}{{∪}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2627}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2628}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2629}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2630}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2631}{}{{p}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2632}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2633}{}{{)}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2634}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2635}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2636}{}{{∗}}}}}}}}{\({Pro}^{\Sigma} \subseteq (\Sigma \cup \Sigma_{p})^{\ast}\)}}}\(\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\subseteq(\Sigma\cup\Sigma_{p})^{\ast}\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-156-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2637}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2638}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2639}{}{{λ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2640}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2641}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2642}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2643}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2644}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2648}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2649}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2650}{}{{α}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2645}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2646}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2647}{}{{i}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-2651}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(\lambda i\alpha\lbrack I_{i}^{\alpha}\rbrack\)}}}\(\lambda i\alpha[I_{i}^{\alpha}]\)
tiene dominio igual a

{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-280-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6797}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6798}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6799}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6800}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6801}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
se detiene, partiendo del estado inicial dado ya que llega a un punto en
el que queda intentando realizar
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-281-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6802}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6803}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6804}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6805}{}{{I}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6816}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6817}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6818}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6819}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6820}{}{{P}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6806}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6807}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6808}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6809}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6810}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6811}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6812}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6813}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6814}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-6815}{}{{1}}}}}}}}}{\(I_{n(\mathcal{P}) + 1}^{\mathcal{P}}\)}}}\(I_{n(\mathcal{P})+1}^{\mathcal{P}}\)
lo cual no es una instrucción. Veamos un ejemplo de no detención. Sea
