\hypertarget{definiciuxf3n-matemuxe1tica-de-detenciuxf3n}{%
\paragraph*{\texorpdfstring{\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20detencionux20deux20unux20programa}{}{}Definición
matemática de
detención}{Definición matemática de detención}}\label{definiciuxf3n-matemuxe1tica-de-detenciuxf3n}}
\addcontentsline{toc}{paragraph}{Definición matemática de detención}

Ahora definiremos matemáticamente el concepto de detención. Cuando la
primer coordenada de
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-290-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7761}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7762}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7763}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7796}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7797}{}{{t}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7798}{}{{~veces}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7764}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7765}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7766}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7795}{}{{{}{}{}{}{}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7767}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7768}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7769}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7770}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7771}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7772}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7773}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7774}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7775}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7776}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7777}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7778}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7779}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7780}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7781}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7782}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7783}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7784}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7785}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7786}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7787}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7788}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7789}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7790}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7791}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7792}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7793}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7794}{}{{(}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7799}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7800}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7801}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7802}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7803}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7805}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7804}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7806}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7807}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7808}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7809}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7811}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7810}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7812}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7813}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7814}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7815}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7816}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7817}{}{{)}}}}{\[\overset{t\text{~veces}}{\overbrace{S_{\mathcal{P}}(...S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(}}1,\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma}))...)\]}}}}\[\overset{t\text{
veces}}{\overbrace{S_{\mathcal{P}}(...S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(}}1,\vec{s},\vec{\sigma}))...)\]
sea igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-291-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7818}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7819}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7820}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7821}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7822}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7823}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7824}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7825}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7826}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7827}{}{{1}}}}{\(n(\mathcal{P}) + 1\)}}}\(n(\mathcal{P})+1\),
diremos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-292-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7828}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7829}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7830}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7831}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7832}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
\emph{se detiene (luego de}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-293-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7833}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7834}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7835}{}{{t}}}}{\(t\)}}}\(t\)
\emph{pasos), partiendo desde el estado}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-294-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7836}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7837}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7838}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7839}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7840}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7841}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7843}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7842}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7844}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7845}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7846}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7847}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7849}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7848}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7850}{}{{)}}}}{\((\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma})\)}}}\((\vec{s},\vec{\sigma})\).
Si ninguna de las primeras coordenadas en la computación
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-295-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7851}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7852}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7853}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7854}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7855}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7856}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7857}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7858}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7859}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7861}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7860}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7862}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7863}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7864}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7865}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7867}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7866}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7868}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7869}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7870}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7871}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7872}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7873}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7874}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7875}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7876}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7877}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7878}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7879}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7880}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7881}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7882}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7884}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7883}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7885}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7886}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7887}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7888}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7890}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7889}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7891}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7892}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7893}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7894}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7895}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7896}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7897}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7898}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7899}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7900}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7901}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7902}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7903}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7904}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7905}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7906}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7907}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7908}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7909}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7910}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7911}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7912}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7913}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7915}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7914}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7916}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7917}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7918}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7919}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7921}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7920}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7922}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7923}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7924}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7925}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7926}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7927}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7928}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7929}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7930}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7931}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7932}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7933}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7934}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7935}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7936}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7937}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7938}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7939}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7940}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7941}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7942}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7943}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7944}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7945}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7946}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7947}{}{{P}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7948}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7949}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7950}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7951}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7952}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7953}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7955}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7954}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7956}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7957}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7958}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7959}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7961}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7960}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7962}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7963}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7964}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7965}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7966}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7967}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7968}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7969}{}{{)}}}}{\[((1,\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma}),S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma}),S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma})),S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma}))),...)\]}}}}\[((1,\vec{s},\vec{\sigma}),S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\vec{s},\vec{\sigma}),S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\vec{s},\vec{\sigma})),S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(S_{\mathcal{P}}(1,\vec{s},\vec{\sigma}))),...)\]
es igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-296-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7970}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7971}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7972}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7973}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7974}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7975}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7976}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7977}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7978}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7979}{}{{1}}}}{\(n(\mathcal{P}) + 1\)}}}\(n(\mathcal{P})+1\),
diremos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-297-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7980}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7981}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7982}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7983}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7984}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
\emph{no se detiene partiendo del estado}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-298-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7985}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7986}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7987}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7988}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7989}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7990}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7992}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7991}{}{{s}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7993}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7994}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7995}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7996}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7998}{}{{→}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7997}{}{{σ}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-7999}{}{{)}}}}{\((\overset{\rightarrow}{s},\overset{\rightarrow}{\sigma})\)}}}\((\vec{s},\vec{\sigma})\).
Como puede observarse los programas de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-299-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8000}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8001}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8002}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8003}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8004}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8005}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8006}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8007}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8008}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
tienen una sola manera de detenerse, i.e. siempre que se detienen lo
hacen habiendo realizado la última de sus instrucciones e intentando
realizar la instrucción siguiente a su última instrucción.

Nótese que en los conceptos antes definidos por "1 paso" entendemos
``aplicar una ves la función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-300-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8009}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8010}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8011}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8012}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8013}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8014}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8015}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8016}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8017}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}}{\(S_{\mathcal{P}}\)}}}\(S_{\mathcal{P}}\)''
y esto no siempre involucra ``realizar una instrucción'' ya que podría
pasar que aplicáramos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-301-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8018}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8019}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8020}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8021}{}{{S}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8022}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8023}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8024}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8025}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8026}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}}{\(S_{\mathcal{P}}\)}}}\(S_{\mathcal{P}}\)
a una descripción instantánea cuya primer coordenada es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-302-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8027}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8028}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8029}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8030}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8031}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8032}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8033}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8034}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8035}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8036}{}{{1}}}}{\(n(\mathcal{P}) + 1\)}}}\(n(\mathcal{P})+1\).
Podemos redondear esta idea diciendo que ``1 paso'' equivale a
"realizarp una instrucción", donde tal como se lo explico antes
"realizarp" significa "realizar si se puede".

\hypertarget{funciones-sigma-computables}{%
\subsubsection[{4.3.3} Funciones
\(\Sigma\)-computables]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.3} Funciones
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-303-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8037}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8038}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8039}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computables}{4.3.3 Funciones Σ\textbackslash Sigma\textbackslash Sigma-computables}}\label{funciones-sigma-computables}}

Ahora que hemos definido matemáticamente la semántica de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-304-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8040}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8041}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8042}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8043}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8044}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8045}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8046}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8047}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8048}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
estamos en condiciones de definir el concepto de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-305-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8049}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8050}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8051}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable,
el cual será una modelización matemática del concepto de función
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3.1-funciones-sigma-efectivamente-computables.html\#definicion\%20de\%20funcion\%20sigma-efectivamente\%20computable}{{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-306-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8052}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8053}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8054}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable. Intuitivamente hablando una función será
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-307-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8055}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8056}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8057}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
cuando haya un programa que la compute. Para precisar este concepto nos
será útil la siguiente notación. Dados
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-308-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8058}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8059}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8060}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8061}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8062}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8063}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8064}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8065}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8066}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8067}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8068}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8069}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8070}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8071}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8072}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8073}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8074}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8075}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8076}{}{{ω}}}}{\(x_{1},...,x_{n} \in \omega\)}}}\(x_{1},...,x_{n}\in\omega\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-309-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8077}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8078}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8079}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8080}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8081}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8082}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8083}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8084}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8085}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8086}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8087}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8088}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8089}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8090}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8091}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8092}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8093}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8094}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8095}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8096}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8097}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8098}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8099}{}{{∗}}}}}}}}{\(\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \in \Sigma^{\ast}\)}}}\(\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\in\Sigma^{\ast}\),
con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-310-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8100}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8101}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8102}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8103}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8104}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8105}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8106}{}{{ω}}}}{\(n,m \in \omega\)}}}\(n,m\in\omega\),
usaremos
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-311-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8107}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8108}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8109}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8110}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8111}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8112}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8113}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8114}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8115}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8116}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8117}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8118}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8119}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8120}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8121}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8122}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8123}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8124}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8125}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8126}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8127}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8128}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8129}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8130}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8131}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8132}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8133}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8134}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8135}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8136}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8137}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8138}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8139}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8140}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8141}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8142}{}{{∥}}}}}{\[\left\| x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \right\|\]}}}}\[\left\Vert
x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\right\Vert\] para denotar el
estado
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-312-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8143}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8144}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8145}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8146}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8147}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8148}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8149}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8150}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8151}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8152}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8153}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8154}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8155}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8156}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8157}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8158}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8159}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8160}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8161}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8162}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8163}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8164}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8165}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8166}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8167}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8168}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8169}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8170}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8171}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8172}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8173}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8174}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8175}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8176}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8177}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8178}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8179}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8180}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8181}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8182}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8183}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8184}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8185}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8186}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8187}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8188}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8189}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8190}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8191}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8192}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8193}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8194}{}{{)}}}}}{\[\left( (x_{1},...,x_{n},0,...),(\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m},\varepsilon,...) \right)\]}}}}\[\left((x_{1},...,x_{n},0,...),(\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m},\varepsilon,...)\right)\]
Esta notación requiere aclarar un poco como debe interpretarse en los
casos limite, es decir cuando alguno de los números
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-313-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8195}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8196}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8197}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8198}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8199}{}{{m}}}}{\(n,m\)}}}\(n,m\)
es igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-314-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8200}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8201}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8202}{}{{0}}}}{\(0\)}}}\(0\).
Nótese que por ejemplo
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-315-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8203}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8204}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8205}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8206}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8207}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8208}{}{{∥}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8209}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8210}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8211}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8212}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8213}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8214}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8215}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8216}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8217}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8218}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8219}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8220}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8221}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8222}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8223}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8224}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8225}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8226}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8227}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8228}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8229}{}{{)}}}}}{\[\left\| x \right\| = \left( (x,0,...),(\varepsilon,...) \right)\]}}}}\[\left\Vert x\right\Vert
=\left((x,0,...),(\varepsilon,...)\right)\] (es el caso
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-316-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8230}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8231}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8232}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8233}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8234}{}{{1}}}}{\(n = 1\)}}}\(n=1\)
y

También
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-318-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8240}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8241}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8242}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8243}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8244}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8245}{}{{∥}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8246}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8247}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8248}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8249}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8250}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8251}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8252}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8253}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8254}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8255}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8256}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8257}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8258}{}{{α}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8259}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8260}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8261}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8262}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8263}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8264}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8265}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8266}{}{{)}}}}}{\[\left\| \alpha \right\| = \left( (0,...),(\alpha,\varepsilon,...) \right)\]}}}}\[\left\Vert \alpha\right\Vert
=\left((0,...),(\alpha,\varepsilon,...)\right)\] (es el caso
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-319-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8267}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8268}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8269}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8270}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8271}{}{{0}}}}{\(n = 0\)}}}\(n=0\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-320-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8272}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8273}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8274}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8275}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8276}{}{{1}}}}{\(m = 1\)}}}\(m=1\)).
En el caso
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-321-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8277}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8278}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8279}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8280}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8281}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8282}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8283}{}{{0}}}}{\(n = m = 0\)}}}\(n=m=0\)
pensaremos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-322-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8284}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8285}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8286}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8287}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8288}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8289}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8290}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8291}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8292}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8293}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8294}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8295}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8296}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8297}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8298}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8299}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8300}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8301}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8302}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8303}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8304}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8305}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8306}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8307}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8308}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8309}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8310}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8311}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8312}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8313}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8314}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8315}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8316}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\)}}}\(x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\)
se transforma en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-323-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8317}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8318}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8319}{}{{◊}}}}{\(\lozenge\)}}}\(\lozenge\)
por lo que se obtiene
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-324-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8320}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8321}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8323}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8324}{}{{◊}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8325}{}{{∥}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8326}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8327}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8328}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8329}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8330}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8331}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8332}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8333}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8334}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8335}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8336}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8337}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8338}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8339}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8340}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8341}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8342}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8343}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8344}{}{{)}}}}}{\[\left\| \lozenge \right\| = \left( (0,...),(\varepsilon,...) \right)\]}}}}\[\left\Vert
\lozenge\right\Vert =\left((0,...),(\varepsilon,...)\right)\] Además es
claro que
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-325-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8345}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8346}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8347}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8348}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8349}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8350}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8351}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8352}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8353}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8354}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8355}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8356}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8357}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8358}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8359}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8360}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8361}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8362}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8363}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8364}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8365}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8366}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8367}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8368}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8369}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8370}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8371}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8372}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8373}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8374}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8375}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8376}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8377}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8378}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8379}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8380}{}{{∥}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8381}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8382}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8383}{}{{{∥}{∥
∥}{∥}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8384}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8385}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8386}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8387}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8388}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8389}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8390}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8391}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8392}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8393}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8394}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8395}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8396}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8397}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8398}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8399}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8400}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8413}{}{{i}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8401}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8402}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8403}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8412}{}{{{}{}{}{}{}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8404}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8405}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8406}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8407}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8408}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8409}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8410}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8411}{}{{0}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8414}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8415}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8416}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8417}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8418}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8419}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8420}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8421}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8422}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8423}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8424}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8425}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8426}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8427}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8428}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8429}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8430}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8431}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8444}{}{{j}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8432}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8433}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8434}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8443}{}{{{}{}{}{}{}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8435}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8436}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8437}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8438}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8439}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8440}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8441}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8442}{}{{ε}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8445}{}{{{∥}{∥
∥}{∥}}}}}}{\[\left\| x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \right\| = \left\| x_{1},...,x_{n},\overset{i}{\overbrace{0,...,0}},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m},\overset{j}{\overbrace{\varepsilon,...,\varepsilon}} \right\|\]}}}}\[\left\Vert
x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\right\Vert =\left\Vert
x_{1},...,x_{n},\overset{i}{\overbrace{0,...,0}},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m},\overset{j}{\overbrace{\varepsilon,...,\varepsilon}}\right\Vert\]
cualesquiera sean

Dado
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-327-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8453}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8454}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8455}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8456}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8457}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8458}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8459}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8460}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8461}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8462}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8463}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8464}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8465}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8466}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-8467}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} \in {Pro}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\in\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\),
definamos para cada par

  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-367-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9602}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9603}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9604}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9605}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9606}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9607}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9608}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9609}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9610}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9611}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9612}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9613}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9614}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9615}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9616}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9617}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9618}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9619}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9620}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9621}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9622}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9623}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9624}{}{{)}}}}{\(((0,0,...),(\varepsilon,\varepsilon,...))\)}}}\(((0,0,...),(\varepsilon,\varepsilon,...))\)
  tenemos que
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-368-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9625}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9626}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9627}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9628}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9629}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9630}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9631}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9632}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9638}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9639}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9640}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9641}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9642}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9643}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9644}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9633}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9634}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9635}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9636}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9637}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9645}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9646}{}{{∅}}}}{\(D_{\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{0,0,\#}} = \varnothing\)}}}\(D_{\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{0,0,\#}}=\emptyset\).
\end{enumerate}

Por supuesto para que el concepto de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-369-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9647}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9648}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9649}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
tenga chance de ser una modelización adecuada del concepto de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-370-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9650}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9651}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9652}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable, tiene que ser cierto el siguiente resultado.

\textbf{4.7} (Leibniz vence a Neumann). \emph{Si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-371-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9653}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9654}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9655}{}{{f}}}}{\(f\)}}}}\(f\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-372-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9656}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9657}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9658}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable,
entonces
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-373-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9659}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9660}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9661}{}{{f}}}}{\(f\)}}}\(f\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-374-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9662}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9663}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9664}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable.

\textbf{Proof.} Supongamos por ejemplo que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-375-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9665}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9666}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9667}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9668}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9669}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9670}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9671}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9672}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9673}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9674}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9675}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9676}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9677}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9678}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9679}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9680}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9681}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9682}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9683}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9684}{}{{ω}}}}{\(f:S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\rightarrow\omega\)}}}\(f:S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\rightarrow\omega\) es computada por
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-376-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9685}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9686}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9687}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9688}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9689}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9690}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9691}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9692}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9693}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9694}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9695}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9696}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9697}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9698}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9699}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} \in {Pro}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\in\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\).
Un
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3-procedimientos-efectivos.html\#definicion\%20de\%20procedimiento\%20efectivo}{procedimiento
efectivo} que compute a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-377-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9700}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9701}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9702}{}{{f}}}}{\(f\)}}}\(f\)
puede consistir de realizar las sucesivas instrucciones de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-378-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9703}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9704}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9705}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9706}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9707}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
(partiendo de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-379-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9708}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9709}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9710}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9711}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9712}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9713}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9714}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9715}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9716}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9717}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9718}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9719}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9720}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9721}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9722}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9723}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9724}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9725}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9726}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9727}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9728}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9729}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9730}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9731}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9732}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9733}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9734}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9735}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9736}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9737}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9738}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9739}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9740}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9741}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9742}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9743}{}{{∥}}}}}{\(\left\| x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \right\|\)}}}\(\left\Vert
x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\right\Vert\)) y eventualmente
terminar en caso de que nos toque realizar la instrucción
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-380-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9744}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9745}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9746}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9747}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9748}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9749}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9750}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9751}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9752}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9753}{}{{1}}}}{\(n(\mathcal{P}) + 1\)}}}\(n(\mathcal{P})+1\),
y dar como salida el contenido de la variable
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-381-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9754}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9755}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9756}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9757}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9758}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9759}{}{{1}}}}{\(N1\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}1\).
Daremos a continuación una descripción mas detallada de dicho
procedimiento.

Fijemos primero un número natural
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-382-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9760}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9761}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9762}{}{{k}}}}{\(k\)}}}\(k\)
que sea mayor que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-383-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9763}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9764}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9765}{}{{max}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9766}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9767}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9768}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9769}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9770}{}{{\}}}}}{\(\max\{ n,m\}\)}}}\(\max\{n,m\}\)
y tal que toda variable que ocurre en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-384-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9771}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9772}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9773}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9774}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9775}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
este en la lista
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-385-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9776}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9777}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9778}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9779}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9780}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9781}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9782}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9783}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9784}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9785}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9786}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9787}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9788}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9789}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9790}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9791}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9792}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9794}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9793}{}{{k}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9795}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9796}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9797}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9798}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9799}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9800}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9801}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9802}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9803}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9804}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9805}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9806}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9807}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9808}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9809}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9810}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9812}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9811}{}{{k}}}}}}}}}{\(N1,...,N\overline{k},P1,...,P\overline{k}\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}1,...,\mathrm{N}\bar{k},\mathrm{P}1,...,\mathrm{P}\bar{k}\).
Sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-386-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9813}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9814}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9815}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9816}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9817}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathbb{P}\)}}}\(\mathbb{P}\)
el siguiente procedimiento efectivo:

- Conjunto de datos de entrada de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-387-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9818}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9819}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9820}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9821}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9822}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathbb{P}\)}}}\(\mathbb{P}\)
igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-388-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9823}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9824}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9825}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9826}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9827}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9828}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9829}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9830}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9831}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9832}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9833}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9834}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9835}{}{{∗}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9836}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9837}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9838}{}{}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9839}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9840}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9841}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast}{}^{m}\)}}}\(\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast}{}^{m}\)

- Conjunto de datos de salida de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-389-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9842}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9843}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9844}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9845}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9846}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathbb{P}\)}}}\(\mathbb{P}\)
contenido en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-390-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9847}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9848}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9849}{}{{ω}}}}{\(\omega\)}}}\(\omega\)

- Funcionamiento:

Etapa 1

Asignar los siguientes valores a las variables
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-391-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9850}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9851}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9852}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9853}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9854}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9855}{}{{X}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9856}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9857}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9858}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9859}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9860}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9861}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9862}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9863}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9864}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9865}{}{{X}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9866}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9867}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9868}{}{{k}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9869}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9870}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9871}{}{{A}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9872}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9873}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9874}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9875}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9876}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9877}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9878}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9879}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9880}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9881}{}{{A}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9882}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9883}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9884}{}{{k}}}}}}}}{\(I,X_{1},...,X_{k},A_{1},...,A_{k}\)}}}\(I,X_{1},...,X_{k},A_{1},...,A_{k}\):
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-392-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9885}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9886}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9887}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9888}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9889}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9890}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9891}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9892}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9893}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9894}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9895}{}{{1}}{}}}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9896}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9897}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9898}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9899}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9900}{}{{X}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9901}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9902}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9903}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9904}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9905}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9906}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9907}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9908}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9909}{}{{1}}}}}}{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9910}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9911}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9912}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9913}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9914}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9915}{}{{A}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9916}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9917}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9918}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9919}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9920}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9921}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9922}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9923}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9924}{}{{1}}}}}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9925}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9926}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9927}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9928}{}{{⋮}}{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9929}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-9930}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-99 Etapa 3

Si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-402-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10235}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10236}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10237}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10238}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10239}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10240}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10241}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10242}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10243}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10244}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10245}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10246}{}{{1}}}}{\(I = n(\mathcal{P}) + 1\)}}}\(I=n(\mathcal{P})+1\),
entonces dar
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-403-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10247}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10248}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10249}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10250}{}{{X}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10251}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10252}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10253}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(X_{1}\)}}}\(X_{1}\)
como salida y detenerse. En caso contrario ir a Etapa 2.

Se deja al lector corroborar que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-404-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10254}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10255}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10256}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10257}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10258}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathbb{P}\)}}}\(\mathbb{P}\)
es efectivo. ~

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

Sin embargo nuestro modelo imperativo de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-405-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10259}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10260}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10261}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable todavía podría no ser correcto ya que podría pasar que haya
una función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-406-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10262}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10263}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10264}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-mixta
que sea computada por un procedimiento efectivo pero que no exista un
programa de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-407-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10265}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10266}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10267}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10268}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10269}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10270}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10271}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10272}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10273}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
que la compute. En otras palabras el modelo imperativo o Neumanniano
podría ser incompleto. Por supuesto este no es el caso y los desarrollos
que veremos mas adelante nos convencerán de que el paradigma imperativo
es completo, es decir Neumann también vence a Leibniz.

\hypertarget{macros}{%
\subsubsection[{4.3.4} Macros]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.4}
\protect\hypertarget{macros}{}{}Macros}{4.3.4 Macros}}\label{macros}}

Supongamos que estamos escribiendo un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-408-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10274}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10275}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10276}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10277}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10278}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-409-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10279}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10280}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10281}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10282}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10283}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10284}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10285}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10286}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10287}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
con el objeto de que realice cierta tarea. Supongamos además que nos
vendría muy bien para nuestros propósitos poder usar una instrucción
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-410-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10288}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10289}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10290}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10291}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10292}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10293}{}{{5}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10294}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10295}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10296}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10297}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10298}{}{{16}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10299}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10300}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10301}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10302}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10303}{}{{3}}}}{\[N5\leftarrow N16 + N3\]}}}}\[\mathrm{N}5\leftarrow\mathrm{N}16+\mathrm{N}3\]
la cual por supuesto al correr el programa, debería producir el efecto
de dejar en la variable
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-411-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10304}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10305}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10306}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10307}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10308}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10309}{}{{5}}}}{\(N5\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}5\)
la suma de los contenidos de las variables
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-412-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10310}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10311}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10312}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10313}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10314}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10315}{}{{16}}}}{\(N16\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}16\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-413-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10316}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10317}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10318}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10319}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10320}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10321}{}{{3}}}}{\(N3\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}3\),
sin modificar el contenido de las variables distintas a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-414-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10323}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10324}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10325}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10326}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10327}{}{{5}}}}{\(N5\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}5\).
Lamentablemente no tenemos en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-415-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10328}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10329}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10330}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10331}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10332}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10333}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10334}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10335}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-10336}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
este tipo de instrucción pero podríamos reemplazarla por el siguiente

obtenemos el programa que simulaba la instrucción
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-497-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11333}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11334}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11335}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11336}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11337}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11338}{}{{20}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11339}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11340}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11341}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11342}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11343}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11344}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11345}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11346}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11347}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11348}{}{{14}}}}{\(N20\leftarrow N1 + N14\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}20\leftarrow\mathrm{N}1+\mathrm{N}14\)
dentro de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-498-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11349}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11350}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11351}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11352}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11353}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\).
La practicidad de tener el molde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-499-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11354}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11355}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11356}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
cae de maduro. Ahora en caso de necesitar una instrucción del tipo
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-500-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11357}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11358}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11359}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11360}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11361}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11362}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11363}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11364}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11366}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11365}{}{{k}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11367}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11368}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11369}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11370}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11371}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11372}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11373}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11375}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11374}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11376}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11377}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11378}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11379}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11380}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11381}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11382}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11384}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11383}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\(N\overline{k}\leftarrow N\overline{n} + N\overline{m}\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}\bar{k}\leftarrow\mathrm{N}\bar{n}+\mathrm{N}\bar{m}\)
solo tenemos que reemplazar en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-501-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11385}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11386}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11387}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)

\begin{enumerate}

  - cada ocurrencia de

y reemplazar las "variables"
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-508-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11436}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11437}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11438}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11439}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11440}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11441}{}{{4}}}}{\(V4\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}4\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-509-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11442}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11443}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11444}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11445}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11446}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11447}{}{{5}}}}{\(V5\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}5\)
y los "labels"
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-510-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11448}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11449}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11450}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11451}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11452}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11453}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\),
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-511-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11454}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11455}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11456}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11457}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11458}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11459}{}{{2}}}}{\(A2\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}2\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-512-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11460}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11461}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11462}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11463}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11464}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11465}{}{{3}}}}{\(A3\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}3\),
por dos variables concretas y tres labels concretos que no se usen en el
programa que estamos realizando. El programa así obtenido simulara a la
instrucción
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-513-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11466}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11467}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11468}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11469}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11470}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11471}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11472}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11473}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11475}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11474}{}{{k}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11476}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11477}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11478}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11479}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11480}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11481}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11482}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11484}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11483}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11485}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11486}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11487}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11488}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11489}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11490}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11491}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11493}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11492}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\(N\overline{k}\leftarrow N\overline{n} + N\overline{m}\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}\bar{k}\leftarrow\mathrm{N}\bar{n}+\mathrm{N}\bar{m}\).

En la jerga computacional el molde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-514-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11494}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11495}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11496}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
suele llamarse \emph{macro} y los programas obtenidos luego de realizar
los reemplazos son llamados \emph{expansiones de}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-515-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11497}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11498}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11499}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\).
Nótese que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-516-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11500}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11501}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11502}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11503}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11504}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11505}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11506}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11507}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11508}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11509}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11510}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11511}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11512}{}{{L}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11513}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11514}{}{{B}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11515}{}{{R}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11516}{}{{A}}}}}}{\(Ti(M) = {PALABRA}\)}}}\(Ti(M)=\mathrm{PALABRA}\)
ya que, como en el caso de los programas, escribimos a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-517-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11517}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11518}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11519}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
linea por linea para facilitar su manejo pero en realidad es una sola
palabra, a saber:
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-518-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11520}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11521}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11522}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11523}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11524}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11525}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11526}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11527}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11528}{}{{←}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11529}{}{{V}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11530}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11531}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11532}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11533}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11534}{}{{4}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11535}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11536}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11537}{}{{←}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11538}{}{{V}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11539}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11540}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11541}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11542}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11543}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11544}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11545}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11546}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11547}{}{{F}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11548}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11549}{}{{4}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11550}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11551}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11552}{}{{≠}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11553}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11554}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11555}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11556}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11557}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11558}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11559}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11560}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11561}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11562}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11563}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11564}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11565}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11566}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11567}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11568}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11569}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11570}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11571}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11572}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11573}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11574}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11575}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11576}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11577}{}{{4}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11578}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11579}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11580}{}{{←}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11581}{}{{V}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11582}{}{{4}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11583}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11584}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11585}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11586}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11587}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11589}{}{{˙}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11588}{}{{−}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11590}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11591}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11592}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11593}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11594}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11595}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11596}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11597}{}{{←}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11598}{}{{V}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11599}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11600}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11601}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11602}{}{{+}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11603}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11604}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11605}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11606}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11607}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11608}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11609}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11610}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11611}{}{{1}}\protect\hy
