\neq 0{GOTOA}2{GOTOA}3A2V4\leftarrow\text{V}4\overset{˙}{-}1V1\leftarrow\text{V}1 + 1{GOTOA}1A3{SKIP}\]}}}}\[\mathrm{V}1\mathrm{\leftarrow}\text{V}2\mathrm{V}4\mathrm{\leftarrow}\text{V}3\mathrm{A}1\mathrm{IFV}4\mathrm{\neq}0\mathrm{GOTOA}2\mathrm{GOTOA}3\mathrm{A}2\mathrm{V}4\mathrm{\leftarrow}\text{V}4\mathrm{\dot{-}}1\mathrm{V}1\mathrm{\leftarrow}\text{V}1\mathrm{+}1\mathrm{GOTOA}1\mathrm{A}3\mathrm{SKIP}\]
Es decir, como objeto matemático,
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-519-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11622}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11623}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11624}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
es simplemente una palabra. A las palabras de la forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-520-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11625}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11626}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11627}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11628}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11629}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11630}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11631}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11632}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11634}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11633}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\(V\overline{n}\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}\bar{n}\),
con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-521-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11635}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11636}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11637}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11638}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11639}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11640}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11641}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(n \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(n\in\mathbf{N}\),
las llamaremos \emph{variables numéricas de macro}. A las palabras de la
forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-522-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11642}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11643}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11644}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11645}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11646}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11647}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11648}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11649}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11651}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11650}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\(W\overline{n}\)}}}\(\mathrm{W}\bar{n}\),
con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-523-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11652}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11653}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11654}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11655}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11656}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11657}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11658}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(n \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(n\in\mathbf{N}\),
las llamaremos \emph{variables alfabéticas de macro} y a las palabras de
la forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-524-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11659}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11660}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11661}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11662}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11663}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11664}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11665}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11666}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11668}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11667}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}{\(A\overline{n}\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}\bar{n}\),
con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-525-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11669}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11670}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11671}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11672}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11673}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11674}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11675}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(n \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(n\in\mathbf{N}\),
las llamaremos \emph{labels de macro}. Nuestro macro
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-526-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11676}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11677}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11678}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
no tiene variables alfabéticas de macro pero otros macros por supuesto
pueden tener este tipo de variables.

Las variables
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-527-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11679}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11680}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11681}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11682}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11683}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11684}{}{{1}}}}{\(V1\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}1\),
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-528-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11685}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11686}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11687}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11688}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11689}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11690}{}{{2}}}}{\(V2\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}2\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-529-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11691}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11692}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11693}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11694}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11695}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11696}{}{{3}}}}{\(V3\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}3\)
son llamadas \emph{variables oficiales} de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-530-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11697}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11698}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11699}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
ya que son las variables que serán reemplazadas por variables que son
protagonistas dentro del programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-531-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11700}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11701}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11702}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11703}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11704}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
que usara la expansión de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-532-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11705}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11706}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11707}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\).
Las palabras
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-533-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11708}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11709}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11710}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11711}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11712}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11713}{}{{4}}}}{\(V4\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}4\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-534-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11714}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11715}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11716}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11717}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11718}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11719}{}{{5}}}}{\(V5\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}5\)
son llamadas \emph{variables auxiliares} de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-535-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11720}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11721}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11722}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
ya que serán reemplazadas por variables que se usaran solo dentro de la
expansión y no intervienen en la "trama" del programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-536-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11723}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11724}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11725}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11726}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11727}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\).
También
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-537-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11728}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11729}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11730}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11731}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11732}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11733}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\),
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-538-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11734}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11735}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11736}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11737}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11738}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11739}{}{{2}}}}{\(A2\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}2\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-539-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11740}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11741}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11742}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11743}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11744}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11745}{}{{3}}}}{\(A3\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}3\)
son llamados \emph{labels auxiliares} de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-540-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11746}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11747}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11748}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
ya que son usados solo para su funcionamiento interno y no tienen
vinculación con los labels del programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-541-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11749}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11750}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11751}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11752}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11753}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\).

En el siguiente ejemplo veremos un macro que tiene un label que no es
auxiliar sino oficial. Supongamos que estamos escribiendo un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-542-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11754}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11755}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11756}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11757}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11758}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11759}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11760}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11761}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11762}{}{{′}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}^{\prime}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}^{\prime}\)
y nos hace falta simular instrucciones de la forma
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-543-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11763}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11764}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11765}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11766}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11767}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11768}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11769}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11770}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11771}{}{{\textbar{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11772}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11773}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11774}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11775}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11776}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11777}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11779}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11778}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11780}{}{{\textbar{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11781}{}{{≤}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11782}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11783}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11784}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11785}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11786}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11787}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11789}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11788}{}{{m}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11790}{}{{~}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11791}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11792}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11793}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11794}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11795}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11796}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11797}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11798}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11799}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11800}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11801}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11802}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11803}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11805}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11804}{}{{k}}}}}}}}}{\[{IF}\;\left| P\overline{n} \right| \leq N\overline{m}\ {GOTO}\; L\overline{k}\]}}}}\[\mathrm{IF}\;\left\vert
\mathrm{P}\bar{n}\right\vert \leq\mathrm{N}\bar{m}\
\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{k}\] (por supuesto estas instrucciones no
pertenecen al lenguaje
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-544-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11806}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11807}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11808}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11809}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11810}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11811}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11812}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11813}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11814}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
pero debería quedar claro como funcionan). Construiremos un macro que
nos permita simular dicho tipo de instrucciones. Aquí la construcción
del macro dependerá de quien es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-545-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11815}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11816}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11817}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\),
es decir el macro nos servirá para simular instrucciones de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-546-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11818}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11819}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11820}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11821}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11822}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11823}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11824}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11825}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11826}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
haciendo programas de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-547-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11827}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11828}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11829}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11830}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11831}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11832}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11833}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11834}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11835}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
y si lo usamos haciendo un programa de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-548-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11836}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11837}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11838}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11839}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11840}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11841}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11842}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11843}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11844}{}{{Γ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\),
donde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-549-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11845}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11846}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11847}{}{{Γ}}}}{\(\Gamma\)}}}\(\Gamma\)
es otro alfabeto que contenga a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-550-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11848}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11849}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11850}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\),
el macro no funcionara bien. Haremos entonces el macro para el caso de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-551-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11851}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11852}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11853}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11854}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11855}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11856}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11857}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11858}{}{{@}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11859}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11860}{}{{!}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11861}{}{{\}}}}}{\(\Sigma = \{@,!\}\)}}}\(\Sigma=\{@,!\}\).
Sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-552-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11862}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11863}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11864}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11865}{}{{M}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11866}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11867}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11868}{}{{′}}}}}}}}{\(M^{\prime}\)}}}\(M^{\prime}\)
el siguiente macro:
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-553-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11869}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11870}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11871}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11872}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11873}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11874}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11875}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11876}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11877}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11878}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11879}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11880}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11881}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11882}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11883}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11884}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11885}{}{{1}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11886}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11887}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11888}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11889}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11890}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11891}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11892}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11893}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11894}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11895}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11896}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11897}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11898}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11899}{}{{1}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11900}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11901}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11902}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11903}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11904}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11905}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11906}{}{{4}}{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11907}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11908}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11909}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11910}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11911}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11912}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11913}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-11914}{}{\protect\hyper y

y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-572-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12264}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12265}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12266}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12267}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12268}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12269}{}{{2}}}}{\(V2\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}2\),

de las variables oficiales. Dado que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-573-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12270}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12271}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12272}{}{{Σ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12273}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12274}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12275}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12276}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12277}{}{{@}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12278}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12279}{}{{!}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12280}{}{{\}}}}}{\(\Sigma = \{@,!\}\)}}}\(\Sigma=\{@,!\}\),
las dos siguientes lineas sirven para decidir si el contenido de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-574-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12281}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12282}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12283}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12284}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12285}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12286}{}{{2}}}}{\(W2\)}}}\(\mathrm{W}2\)
es

Es decir
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-621-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12628}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12629}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12630}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12631}{}{{M}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12632}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12633}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12634}{}{{′}}}}}}}}{\(M^{\prime}\)}}}\(M^{\prime}\)
funciona como un molde con el cual haciendo reemplazos adecuados podemos
simular en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-622-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12635}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12636}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12637}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12638}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12639}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12640}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12641}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12642}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12643}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
cualquier instrucción del tipo
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-623-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12644}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12645}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12646}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12647}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12648}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12649}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12650}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12651}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12652}{}{{\textbar{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12653}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12654}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12655}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12656}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12657}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12658}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12660}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12659}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12661}{}{{\textbar{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12662}{}{{≤}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12663}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12664}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12665}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12666}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12667}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12668}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12670}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12669}{}{{m}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12671}{}{{~}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12672}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12673}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12674}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12675}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12676}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12677}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12678}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12679}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12680}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12681}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12682}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12683}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12684}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12686}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12685}{}{{k}}}}}}}}}{\({IF}\;\left| P\overline{n} \right| \leq N\overline{m}\ {GOTO}\; L\overline{k}\)}}}\(\mathrm{IF}\;\left\vert
\mathrm{P}\bar{n}\right\vert \leq\mathrm{N}\bar{m}\
\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{k}\), con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-624-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12687}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12688}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12689}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12690}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12691}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12692}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12693}{}{{k}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12694}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12695}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12696}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12697}{}{{N}}}}}}{\(n,m,k \in \mathbf{N}\)}}}\(n,m,k\in\mathbf{N}\).

Debería quedar claro el carácter oficial del label
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-625-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12698}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12699}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12700}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12701}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12702}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12703}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\)
en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-626-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12704}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12705}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12706}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12707}{}{{M}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12708}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12709}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12710}{}{{′}}}}}}}}{\(M^{\prime}\)}}}\(M^{\prime}\)
ya que el label por el que se lo reemplaza para hacer la expansión es
uno de los labels protagonistas del programa que se esta escribiendo.

Cabe destacar que las expansiones de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-627-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12711}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12712}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12713}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12714}{}{{M}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12715}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12716}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12717}{}{{′}}}}}}}}{\(M^{\prime}\)}}}\(M^{\prime}\)
no son programas ya que si bien son concatenaciones de instrucciones, no
cumplen la ley de los GOTO (llamada (G) en la definición de programa)
respecto del label que reemplazo a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-628-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12718}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12719}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12720}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12721}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12722}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12723}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\).

Como se vio en este último ejemplo es importante tener en cuenta que
cuando construimos un macro lo hacemos relativo a un alfabeto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-629-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12724}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12725}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12726}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)
previamente fijado, es decir estamos pensando que dicho macro será usado
para hacer programas de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-630-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12727}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12728}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12729}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12730}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12731}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12732}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12733}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12734}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12735}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
y podría pasar que si lo usáramos para hacer un programa de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-631-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12736}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12737}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12738}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12739}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12740}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12741}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12742}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12743}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12744}{}{{Γ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\),
donde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-632-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12745}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12746}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12747}{}{{Γ}}}}{\(\Gamma\)}}}\(\Gamma\)
es otro alfabeto, el macro no cumpla las propiedades esperadas. Para
visualizar esto mejor, nótese que la palabra
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-633-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12748}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12749}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12750}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12751}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12752}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12753}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12754}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12755}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12756}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12757}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12758}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12759}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12760}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12761}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12762}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12763}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12764}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12765}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12766}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12767}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12768}{}{{B}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12769}{}{{E}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12770}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12771}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12772}{}{{N}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12773}{}{{S}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12774}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12775}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12776}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12777}{}{{@}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12778}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12779}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12780}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12781}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12782}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12783}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12784}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12785}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12786}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12787}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12788}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12789}{}{{2}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12790}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12791}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12792}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12793}{}{\protec  & {{IF}\; W1\;{BEGINS}\;@\;{GOTO}\; A2} \\
 & {{IF}\; W1\;{BEGINS}\;\%\;{GOTO}\; A2} \\
 & {{IF}\; W1\;{BEGINS}\;!\;{GOTO}\; A2} \\
 & {{IF}\; W1\;{BEGINS}\; \uparrow \;{GOTO}\; A2} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; A1} \\
{A2} & {SKIP}
\end{matrix}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{ll}
&
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{W}1\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;@\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}2\\
&
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{W}1\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;\%\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}2\\
&
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{W}1\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;!\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}2\\
&
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{W}1\;\mathrm{BEGINS}\;\uparrow\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}2\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\\
\mathrm{A}2 & \mathrm{SKIP}
\end{array}\] es un macro de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-634-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12932}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12933}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12934}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12935}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12936}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12937}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12938}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12939}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12940}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12941}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12942}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12943}{}{{@}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12944}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12945}{}{{\%}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12946}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12947}{}{{!}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12948}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12949}{}{{↑}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12950}{}{{\}}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\{@,\%,!, \uparrow \}}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\{@,\%,!,\uparrow\}}\)
que simula instrucciones de la forma
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-635-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12951}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12952}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12953}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12954}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12955}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12956}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12957}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12958}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12959}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12960}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12961}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12962}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12963}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12965}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12964}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12966}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12967}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12968}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12969}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12970}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12971}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12972}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12973}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12974}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12975}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12976}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12977}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12978}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12979}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12980}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12981}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12983}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12982}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\[{IF}\; P\overline{n} = \varepsilon\;{GOTO}\; L\overline{m}\]}}}}\[\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{P}\bar{n}=\varepsilon\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}\bar{m}\]
(el cual obviamente podríamos denotar con
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-636-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12984}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12985}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12986}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12987}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12988}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12989}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12990}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12991}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12992}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12993}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12994}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12995}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12996}{}{{ε}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12997}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12998}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-12999}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13000}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13001}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13002}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13003}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13004}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13005}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13006}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13007}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13008}{}{{1}}}}{\({IF}\; W1 = \varepsilon\;{GOTO}\; A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{W}1=\varepsilon\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\)),
pero es claro que esta palabra no nos servirá para simular este tipo de
instrucciones en el lenguaje
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-637-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13009}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13010}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13011}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13012}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13013}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13014}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13015}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13016}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13017}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13018}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13019}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13020}{}{{@}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13021}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13022}{}{{\%}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13023}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13024}{}{{!}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13025}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13026}{}{{↑}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13027}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13028}{}{{△}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13029}{}{{\}}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\{@,\%,!, \uparrow , \bigtriangleup \}}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\{@,\%,!,\uparrow,\vartriangle\}}\).

\textbf{Nota:} Siempre supondremos que la primera instrucción de los
macros no es labelada. Esto es porque muchas veces cuando expandamos un
macro nos interesara labelar la primera instrucción de dicha expansión.
Por supuesto, esto es fácil de conseguir ya que si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-638-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13030}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13031}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13032}{}{{M}}}}{\(M\)}}}\(M\)
es un macro, entonces
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-639-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13033}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13034}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13035}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13036}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13037}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13038}{}{{K}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13039}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13040}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13041}{}{{M}}}}{\({SKIP}M\)}}}\(\mathrm{SKIP}M\)
es también un macro que posee las mismas propiedades.

Como hemos visto recién hay dos tipos de macros:

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  - los de asignación que cuando son expandidos nos dan un programa que
  simula la asignación a una variable dada del resultado de aplicar una
  función a los contenidos de ciertas otras variables; y
\item
  - los de tipo IF que cuando son expandidos nos dan un programa salvo
  por la ley (G), el cual direcciona al label que fue a reemplazar a
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-640-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13042}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13043}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13044}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13045}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13046}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13047}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\)
  cuando se cumple cierta propiedad
  (\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/1.12-funciones-y-conjuntos-sigma-mixtos.html\#definicion\%20de\%20predicado\%20sigma-mixto}{predicado})
  relativa a los contenidos de las variables que fueron a reemplazar a
  las variables oficiales.
\end{enumerate}

\hypertarget{ejemplo-concreto-de-uso-de-macros}{%
\paragraph{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.4.1} Ejemplo concreto de uso de
macros}{4.3.4.1 Ejemplo concreto de uso de macros}}\label{ejemplo-concreto-de-uso-de-macros}}

Ya vimos recién que la palabra

MJXc-Node-13188}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13189}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13190}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13191}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13192}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13193}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13194}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13195}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13196}{}{{1}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13197}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13198}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13199}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13200}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13201}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13202}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13203}{}{{3}}{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13204}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13205}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13206}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13207}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13208}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13209}{}{{K}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13210}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13211}{}{{P}}}}{}}}}}}}}{\[\begin{matrix}
 & {V4\leftarrow V2} \\
 & {V5\leftarrow V3} \\
 & {V1\leftarrow V4} \\
{A1} & {{IF}\; V5 \neq 0\;{GOTO}\; A2} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; A3} \\
{A2} & {V5\leftarrow V5\overset{˙}{-}1} \\
 & {V1\leftarrow V1 + 1} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; A1} \\
{A3} & {SKIP}
\end{matrix}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{ll}
& \mathrm{V}4\leftarrow\mathrm{V}2\\
& \mathrm{V}5\leftarrow\mathrm{V}3\\
& \mathrm{V}1\leftarrow\mathrm{V}4\\
\mathrm{A}1 &
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{V}5\neq0\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}2\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}3\\
\mathrm{A}2 & \mathrm{V}5\leftarrow\mathrm{V}5\dot{-}1\\
& \mathrm{V}1\leftarrow\mathrm{V}1+1\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\\
\mathrm{A}3 & \mathrm{SKIP}
\end{array}\] es un macro que sirve para simular instrucciones de la
forma
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-642-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13212}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13213}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13214}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13215}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13216}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13217}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13218}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13219}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13221}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13220}{}{{k}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13222}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13223}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13224}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13225}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13226}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13227}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13228}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13230}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13229}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13231}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13232}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13233}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13234}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13235}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13236}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13237}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13239}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13238}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\(N\overline{k}\leftarrow N\overline{n} + N\overline{m}\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}\bar{k}\leftarrow\mathrm{N}\bar{n}+\mathrm{N}\bar{m}\)
en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-643-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13240}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13241}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13242}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13243}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13244}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13245}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13246}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13247}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13248}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
(este macro sirve cualquiera sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-644-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13249}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13250}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13251}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)).
Notemos que este macro es de asignación ya que cuando es expandido nos
da un programa que simula la asignación a una variable dada del
resultado de aplicar una función a los contenidos de ciertas otras
variables. En este caso la función es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-645-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13252}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13253}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13254}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13255}{}{{U}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13256}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13257}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13258}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13259}{}{{λ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13260}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13261}{}{{y}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13262}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13263}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13264}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13265}{}{{y}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13266}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(SUMA = \lambda xy\lbrack x + y\rbrack\)}}}\(SUMA=\lambda xy[x+y]\)
por lo cual usaremos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-646-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13267}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13268}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13269}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13270}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13271}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13272}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13273}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13274}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13275}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13276}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13277}{}{{U}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13278}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13279}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13280}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13281}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13282}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13283}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13284}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13285}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13286}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13287}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13288}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13289}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13290}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13291}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\(\left\lbrack V1\leftarrow SUMA(V2,V3) \right\rbrack\)}}}\(\left[\mathrm{V}1\leftarrow
SUMA(\mathrm{V}2,\mathrm{V}3)\right]\) para denotar a dicho macro.
Usaremos este macro para dar un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-647-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13292}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13293}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13294}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13295}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13296}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
que compute a la función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-648-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13297}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13298}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13299}{}{{λ}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13300}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13301}{}{{y}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13302}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13303}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13304}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13305}{}{{y}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13306}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(\lambda xy\lbrack x.y\rbrack\)}}}\(\lambda xy[x.y]\).
Nótese que podemos tomar
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-649-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13307}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13308}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13309}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13310}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13311}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
igual al siguiente programa
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-650-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13312}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13313}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13314}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13315}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13316}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13317}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13318}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13319}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13320}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13321}{}{{1}}{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13323}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13324}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13325}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13326}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13327}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13328}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13329}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13330}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13331}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13332}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13333}{}{{≠}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13334}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13335}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13336}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13337}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13338}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13339}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13340}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13341}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13342}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13343}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13344}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13345}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13346}{}{{2}}{}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13347}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13348}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13349}{}{{}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13350}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13351}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13352}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13353}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13354}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13355}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13356}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13357}{}{{O}}}}\prot {L1} & {{IF}\; N2 \neq 0\;{GOTO}\; L2} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; L3} \\
{L2} & \left\lbrack N3\leftarrow SUMA(N3,N1) \right\rbrack \\
 & {N2\leftarrow N2\overset{˙}{-}1} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; L1} \\
{L3} & {N1\leftarrow N3}
\end{matrix}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{ll}
\mathrm{L}1 &
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{N}2\neq0\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}2\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}3\\
\mathrm{L}2 & \left[\mathrm{N}3\leftarrow
SUMA(\mathrm{N}3,\mathrm{N}1)\right]\\
& \mathrm{N}2\leftarrow\mathrm{N}2\dot{-}1\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}1\\
\mathrm{L}3 & \mathrm{N}1\leftarrow\mathrm{N}3
\end{array}\] donde
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-651-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13449}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13450}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13451}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13452}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13453}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13454}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13455}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13456}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13457}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13458}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13459}{}{{U}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13460}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13461}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13462}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13463}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13464}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13465}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13466}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13467}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13468}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13469}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13470}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13471}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13472}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13473}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\(\left\lbrack N3\leftarrow SUMA(N3,N1) \right\rbrack\)}}}\(\left[\mathrm{N}3\leftarrow
SUMA(\mathrm{N}3,\mathrm{N}1)\right]\) es una expansión del macro
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-652-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13474}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13475}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13476}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13477}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13478}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13479}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13480}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13481}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13482}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13483}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13484}{}{{U}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13485}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13486}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13487}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13488}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13489}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13490}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13491}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13492}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13493}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13494}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13495}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13496}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13497}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13498}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\(\left\lbrack V1\leftarrow SUMA(V2,V3) \right\rbrack\)}}}\(\left[\mathrm{V}1\leftarrow
SUMA(\mathrm{V}2,\mathrm{V}3)\right]\) hecha haciendo el reemplazo de
las variables oficiales
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-653-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13499}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13500}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13501}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13502}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13503}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13504}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13505}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13506}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13507}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13508}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13509}{}{{2}}}}{\(V1,V2\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}1,\mathrm{V}2\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-654-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13510}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13511}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13512}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13513}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13514}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13515}{}{{3}}}}{\(V3\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}3\)
por
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-655-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13516}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13517}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13518}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13519}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13520}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13521}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13522}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13523}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13524}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13525}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13526}{}{{3}}}}{\(N3,N3\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}3,\mathrm{N}3\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-656-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13527}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13528}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13529}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13530}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13531}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13532}{}{{1}}}}{\(N1\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}1\),
respectivamente, y haciendo reemplazos adecuados de sus variables y
labels auxiliares. Hay muchas formas de hacer los reemplazos de
variables y labels auxiliares pero en general no lo especificaremos
explícitamente cuando expandamos un macro ya que es fácil imaginar como
hacerlo en función del programa que estemos realizando. Por ejemplo en
el caso de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-657-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13533}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13534}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13535}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13536}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13537}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
podríamos hacer los siguientes reemplazos:

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  - cada ocurrencia de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-658-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13538}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13539}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13540}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13541}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13542}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13543}{}{{4}}}}{\(V4\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}4\)
  por
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-659-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13544}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13545}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13546}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13547}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13548}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13549}{}{{1111}}}}{\(N1111\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}1111\)
\item
  - cada ocurrencia de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-660-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13550}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13551}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13552}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13553}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13554}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13555}{}{{5}}}}{\(V5\)}}}\(\mathrm{V}5\)
  por
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-661-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13556}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13557}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13558}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13559}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13560}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13561}{}{{2222}}}}{\(N2222\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}2222\)
\item
  - cada ocurrencia de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-662-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13562}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13563}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13564}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13565}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13566}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13567}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\)
  por
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-663-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13568}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13569}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13570}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13571}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13572}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13573}{}{{1000}}}}{\(L1000\)}}}\(\mathrm{L}1000\)
\item
  - cada ocurrencia de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-664-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13574}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13575}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13576}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13577}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13578}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13579}{}{{2}}}}{\(A2\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}2\)
  por
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-665-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13580}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13581}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13582}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13583}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13584}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13585}{}{{2000}}}}{\(L2000\)}}}\(\mathrm{L}2000\)
\item
  - cada ocurrencia de
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-666-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13586}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13587}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13588}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13589}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13590}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13591}{}{{3}}}}{\(A3\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}3\)
  por
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-667-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13592}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13593}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13594}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13595}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13596}{}{{L}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13597}{}{{3000}}}}{\(L3000\)}}}\(\mathrm{L}3000\)
\end{enumerate}

y claramente esto no afectara la "lógica" o "idea" de nuestro programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-668-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13598}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13599}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13600}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13601}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13602}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\).
De esta forma la expansión
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-669-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13603}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13604}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13605}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13606}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13607}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13608}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13609}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13610}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13611}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13612}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13613}{}{{U}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13614}{}{{M}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13615}{}{{A}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13616}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13617}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13618}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13619}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13620}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13621}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13622}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13623}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13624}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13625}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13626}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-13627}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\(\left\lbrack N3\leftarrow SUMA(N3,N1) \right\rbrack\)}}}\(\left[\mathrm{N}3\leftarrow

 & {{GOTO}\; L3} \\
{L2} & {N1111\leftarrow N1} \\
 & {N2222\leftarrow N3} \\
 & {N3\leftarrow N1111} \\
{L1000} & {{IF}\; N2222 \neq 0\;{GOTO}\; L2000} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; L3000} \\
{L2000} & {N2222\leftarrow N2222\overset{˙}{-}1} \\
 & {N3\leftarrow N3 + 1} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; L1000} \\
{L3000} & {SKIP} \\
 & {N2\leftarrow N2\overset{˙}{-}1} \\
 & {{GOTO}\; L1} \\
{L3} & {N1\leftarrow N3}
\end{matrix}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{ll}
\mathrm{L}1 &
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{N}2\neq0\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}2\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}3\\
\mathrm{L}2 & \mathrm{N}1111\leftarrow\mathrm{N}1\\
& \mathrm{N}2222\leftarrow\mathrm{N}3\\
& \mathrm{N}3\leftarrow\mathrm{N}1111\\
\mathrm{L}1000 &
\mathrm{IF}\;\mathrm{N}2222\neq0\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}2000\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}3000\\
\mathrm{L}2000 & \mathrm{N}2222\leftarrow\mathrm{N}2222\dot{-}1\\
& \mathrm{N}3\leftarrow\mathrm{N}3+1\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}1000\\
\mathrm{L}3000 & \mathrm{SKIP}\\
& \mathrm{N}2\leftarrow\mathrm{N}2\dot{-}1\\
& \mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{L}1\\
\mathrm{L}3 & \mathrm{N}1\leftarrow\mathrm{N}3
\end{array}\] el cual por supuesto esta escrito con espacios y en forma
vertical pero es una mera palabra.

\paragraph[{4.3.4.2} Macros asociados a funciones

Dada una función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-674-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14070}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14071}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14072}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14073}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14074}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14075}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14076}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14077}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14078}{}{{f}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14079}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14080}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14081}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14082}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14083}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14084}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14085}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14086}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14087}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14088}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14089}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14090}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14091}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14092}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14093}{}{{ω}}}}{\(f:D_{f} \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\rightarrow\omega\)}}}\(f:D_{f}\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\rightarrow\omega\), usaremos
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-675-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14094}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14095}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14096}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14097}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14098}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14099}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14100}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14101}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14106}{}{{{¯}{¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯}{¯}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14102}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14103}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14104}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14105}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14107}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14108}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14109}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14110}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14111}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14112}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14113}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14114}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14115}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14116}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14117}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14118}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14119}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14120}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14121}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14122}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14123}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14124}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14126}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14125}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14127}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14128}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14129}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14130}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14131}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14132}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14133}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14134}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14135}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14136}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14137}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14 para denotar un macro de

{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-678-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14159}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14160}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14161}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14162}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14163}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14164}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14165}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14166}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14167}{}{{f}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14168}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14169}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14170}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14171}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14172}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14173}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14174}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14175}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14176}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14177}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14178}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14179}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14180}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14181}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14182}{}{{ω}}}}{\(f:D_{f} \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\rightarrow\omega\)}}}\(f:D_{f}\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast

\begin{enumerate}

  no tiene labels oficiales

  \begin{enumerate}

    (elegidas libremente, es decir los números

    son cualesquiera)

        en los valores que le asigna a

        o a las variables que fueron a reemplazar a las variables

        al correr

        desde el estado

        no se modificaran, salvo cuando
        {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-711-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14843}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14844}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14845}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14846}{}{{k}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14847}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14848}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14849}{}{{i}}}}}}}}{\(k_{i}\)}}}\(k_{i}\)
        es igual a
        {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-712-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14850}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14851}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14852}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14853}{}{{k}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14854}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14855}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14856}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14857}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14858}{}{{1}}}}}}}}{\(k_{n + 1}\)}}}\(k_{n+1}\),
        situación en la cual el valor final de
        {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-713-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14859}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14860}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14861}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14862}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14863}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14864}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14870}{}{{{¯}{¯¯}{¯}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14865}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14866}{}{{k}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14867}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14868}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14869}{}{{i}}}}}}}}}}}{\(N\overset{¯}{k_{i}}\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}\overline{k_{i}}\)
        será
        {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-714-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14871}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14872}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14873}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14874}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14875}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14876}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14877}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14878}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14879}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14880}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14881}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14882}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14883}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14884}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14885}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14886}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14887}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14888}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14889}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14890}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14891}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14892}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14893}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14894}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14895}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14896}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14897}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14898}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14899}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14900}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14901}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14902}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14903}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14904}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14905}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14906}{}{{)}}}}{\(f(x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m})\)}}}\(f(x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m})\)

    \item
      (ii) Si
      {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-715-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14907}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14908}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14909}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14910}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14911}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14912}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14913}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14914}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14915}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14916}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14917}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14918}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14919}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14920}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14921}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14922}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14923}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14924}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14925}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14926}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14927}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14928}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14929}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14930}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14931}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14932}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14933}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14934}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14935}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14936}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14937}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14938}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14939}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14940}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14941}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14942}{}{{∉}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14943}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14944}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14945}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14946}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-14947}{}{{f}}}}}}}}{\((x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}) \notin D_{f}\)}}}\((x_{1},...,x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m})\notin

El programa

es comúnmente llamado la \emph{expansión} del macro

con respecto a la elección de variables y labels realizada.

También, dada una función

resulta una función

{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-738-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15452}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15453}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15454}{}{{Γ}}}}{\(\Gamma\)}}}\(\Gamma\)-mixta
y debería quedar claro que no es lo mismo hacer el macro
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-739-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15455}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15456}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15457}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15458}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15459}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15460}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15461}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15462}{}{{3}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15463}{}{{←}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15464}{}{{f}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15465}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15466}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15467}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15468}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15469}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15470}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15471}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15472}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15473}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15474}{}{{2}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15475}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15476}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\[\left\lbrack W3\leftarrow f(W1,W2) \right\rbrack\]}}}}\[\left[\mathrm{W}3\leftarrow
f(\mathrm{W}1,\mathrm{W}2)\right]\] para
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-740-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15477}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15478}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15479}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15480}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15481}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15482}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15483}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15484}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15485}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
que hacerlo para
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-741-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15486}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15487}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15488}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15489}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15490}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15491}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15492}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15493}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15494}{}{{Γ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Gamma}\).

no se especifica quienes son las variables y labels auxiliares de tipo

\textbf{Proof.} Probaremos (b) La prueba de (a) es similar. Sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-752-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15783}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15784}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15785}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15786}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15787}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
un programa que compute a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-753-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15788}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15789}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15790}{}{{f}}}}{\(f\)}}}\(f\).
Tomemos un
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-754-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15791}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15792}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15793}{}{{k}}}}{\(k\)}}}\(k\)
tal que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-755-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15794}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15795}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15796}{}{{k}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15797}{}{{≥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15798}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15799}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15800}{}{{m}}}}{\(k \geq n,m\)}}}\(k\geq n,m\)
y tal que todas las variables y labels de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-756-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15801}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15802}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15803}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15804}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-15805}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
están en el conjunto

{V\overset{¯}{n + 1}\leftarrow V1} \\
{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \  \vdots} \\
{V\overset{¯}{n + n}\leftarrow V\overset{¯}{n}} \\
{V\overset{¯}{n + n + 1}\leftarrow 0} \\
{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \  \vdots} \\
{V\overset{¯}{n + k}\leftarrow 0} \\
{W\overset{¯}{m + 1}\leftarrow W1} \\
{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \  \vdots} \\
{W\overset{¯}{m + m}\leftarrow W\overset{¯}{m}} \\
{W\overset{¯}{m + m + 1}\leftarrow\varepsilon} \\
{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \  \vdots} \\
{W\overset{¯}{m + k}\leftarrow\varepsilon} \\
\mathcal{P}^{\prime}
\end{array}\]}}}}\[\begin{array}{l}
\mathrm{V}\overline{n+1}\leftarrow\mathrm{V}1\\
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \vdots\\
\mathrm{V}\overline{n+n}\leftarrow\mathrm{V}\overline{n}\\
\mathrm{V}\overline{n+n+1}\leftarrow0\\
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \vdots\\
\mathrm{V}\overline{n+k}\leftarrow0\\
\mathrm{W}\overline{m+1}\leftarrow\mathrm{W}1\\
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \vdots\\
\mathrm{W}\overline{m+m}\leftarrow\mathrm{W}\overline{m}\\
\mathrm{W}\overline{m+m+1}\leftarrow\varepsilon\\
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \vdots\\
\mathrm{W}\overline{m+k}\leftarrow\varepsilon\\
\mathcal{P}^{\prime}
\end{array}\] es el macro buscado, el cual tendrá sus variables
auxiliares y labels en la lista

+ 1},...,V\overset{¯}{n + k},W\overset{¯}{m + 2},...,W\overset{¯}{m + k},A1,...,A\overset{¯}{k}.\]}}}}\[\mathrm{V}\overline{n+1},...,\mathrm{V}\overline{n+k},\mathrm{W}\overline{m+2},...,\mathrm{W}\overline{m+k},\mathrm{A}1,...,\mathrm{A}\overline{k}.\]
~

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

decir que si

hay un macro

de

el cual cumpla las siguientes propiedades (no siempre existirá dicho

{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-781-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16419}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16420}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16421}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16422}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16423}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16424}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16425}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16426}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16427}{}{{P}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16428}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16429}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16430}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16431}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16432}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16433}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16434}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16435}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16436}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16437}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16438}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16439}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16440}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16441}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-16442}{}{{ω}}}}{\(P:D_{P} \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\rightarrow\omega\)}}}\(P:D_{P}\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast

= \left\lbrack {IF\ }P(N\overset{¯}{k_{1}},...,N\overset{¯}{k_{n}},P\overset{¯}{j_{1}},...,P\overset{¯}{j_{m}})\ {GOTO\ L}\overline{k} \right\rbrack\)}}}\(\mathcal{E}=\left[\mathrm{IF\
}P(\mathrm{N}\overline{k_{1}},...,\mathrm{N}\overline{k_{n}},\mathrm{P}\overline{j_{1}},...,\mathrm{P}\overline{j_{m}})\
\mathrm{GOTO\ L}\bar{k}\right]\) es llamada la \emph{expansión} del
macro con respecto a la elección de variables y labels realizada. Al
igual que en el caso de los macros de asignación, la notación
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-827-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17252}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17253}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17254}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17255}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17256}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17257}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17258}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17259}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17260}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17261}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17262}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17263}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17264}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17265}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17266}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17267}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17268}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17269}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17270}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17271}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17272}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17273}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17274}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17275}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17276}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17277}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17279}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17278}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17280}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17281}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17282}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17283}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17284}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17285}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17286}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17287}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17288}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17289}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17290}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17291}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17292}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17293}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17294}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17295}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17297}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget tiene cierta ambigüedad ya que no explicita el alfabeto ni los labels y
variables auxiliares de tipo macro.

hay un macro

Nótese que la palabra
