V\overset{¯}{n + 1}\leftarrow P(V1,...,V\overline{n},W1,...,W\overline{m}) \right\rbrack{IFV}\overset{¯}{n + 1} \neq 0{GOTOA}1\]}}}}\[\left[\mathrm{V}\overline{n+1}\leftarrow
P(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\right]\mathrm{IFV}\overline{n+1}\mathrm{\neq}0\mathrm{GOTOA}1\]
es el macro buscado. ~

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

Dejamos al lector probar la reciproca de la proposición anterior, es
decir si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-835-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17546}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17547}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17548}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17549}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17550}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17551}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17552}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17553}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17554}{}{{P}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17555}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17556}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17557}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17558}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17559}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17560}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17561}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17562}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17563}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17564}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17565}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17566}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17567}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17568}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17569}{}{{ω}}}}{\(P:D_{P} \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\rightarrow\omega\)}}}\(P:D_{P}\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\rightarrow\omega\) es tal que en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-836-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17570}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17571}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17572}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17573}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17574}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17575}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17576}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17577}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17578}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
hay un macro
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-837-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17579}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17580}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17581}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17582}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17583}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17584}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17585}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17586}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17587}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17588}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17589}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17590}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17591}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17592}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17593}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17594}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17595}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17596}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17597}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17598}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17599}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17600}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17601}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17602}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17603}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17604}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17606}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17605}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17607}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17608}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17609}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17610}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17611}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17612}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17613}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17614}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17615}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17616}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17617}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17618}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17619}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17620}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17621}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17622}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17624}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17623}{}{{m}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17625}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17626}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17627}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17628}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17629}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17630}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17631}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17632}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17633}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17634}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17635}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17636}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17637}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17638}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\[\left\lbrack {IF}\; P(V1,...,V\overline{n},W1,...,W\overline{m})\;{GOTO}\; A1 \right\rbrack\]}}}}\[\left[\mathrm{IF}\;P(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\right]\]
entonces
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-838-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17639}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17640}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17641}{}\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}
& \left[\mathrm{V}\overline{n+1}\leftarrow
f(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\right]\\
& \left[\mathrm{W}\overline{m+1}\leftarrow
g(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\right]\\
&
\left[\mathrm{IF}\;P(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\right]
\end{aligned}\]

Básicamente habrá dos manantiales de macros de donde obtendremos todos
los macros que potenciaran nuestro lenguaje
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-845-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17948}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17949}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17950}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17951}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17952}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17953}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17954}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17955}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17956}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\).
El
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/4.4-batallas-entre-paradigmas.html\#segundo\%20manantial\%20de\%20macros}{Segundo
Manantial de Macros} es consecuencia del primero y de la batalla
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/4.4-batallas-entre-paradigmas.html\#Neumann\%20vence\%20a\%20Godel}{Neumann
vence a Godel}.

\hypertarget{conjuntos-sigma-enumerables}{%
\subsubsection[{4.3.5} Conjuntos
\(\Sigma\)-enumerables]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.5}
\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20conjuntoux20sigma-enumerable}{}{}Conjuntos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-846-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17957}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17958}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17959}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-enumerables}{4.3.5 Conjuntos Σ\textbackslash Sigma\textbackslash Sigma-enumerables}}\label{conjuntos-sigma-enumerables}}

Ya que la noción de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-847-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17960}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17961}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17962}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
es el modelo matemático Neumanniano o imperativo del concepto de función
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3.1-funciones-sigma-efectivamente-computables.html\#definicion\%20de\%20funcion\%20sigma-efectivamente\%20computable}{{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-848-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17963}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17964}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17965}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable, nos podríamos preguntar entonces cual es el modelo
matemático Neumanniano del concepto de conjunto
\protect\hyperlink{definicionux5cux2520deux5cux2520funcionux5cux2520sigma-efectivamenteux5cux2520enumerable}{{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-849-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17966}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17967}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17968}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
enumerable. Si prestamos atención a la definición de este concepto,
notaremos que depende de la existencia de ciertas funciones
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-850-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17969}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17970}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17971}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computables por lo cual la siguiente definición cae de maduro:

Un conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-851-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17972}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17973}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17974}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17975}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17976}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17977}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17978}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17979}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17980}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17981}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17982}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17983}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17984}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17985}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17986}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17987}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast m}\)
será llamado
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-852-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17988}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17989}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17990}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)\emph{-enumerable}
cuando sea vacío o haya una función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-853-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17991}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17992}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17993}{}{{F}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17994}{}{{:}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17995}{}{{ω}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17996}{}{{→}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17997}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17998}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-17999}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18000}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18001}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18002}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18003}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18004}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18005}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18006}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18007}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18008}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(F:\omega\rightarrow\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(F:\omega\rightarrow\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\) tal que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-854-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18009}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18010}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18011}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18012}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18013}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18014}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18015}{}{{F}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18016}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18017}{}{{S}}}}{\(I_{F} = S\)}}}\(I_{F}=S\)
y
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-855-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18018}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18019}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18020}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18021}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18022}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18023}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18024}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18025}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18026}{}{{)}}}}}}}}{\(F_{(i)}\)}}}\(F_{(i)}\)
sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-856-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18027}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18028}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18029}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable,
para cada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-857-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18030}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18031}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18032}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18033}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18034}{}{{\{}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18035}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18036}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18037}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18038}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18039}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18040}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18041}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18042}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18043}{}{{m}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18044}{}{{\}}}}}{\(i \in \{ 1,...,n + m\}\)}}}\(i\in\{1,...,n+m\}\).

Debería entonces quedar claro que si el concepto de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-858-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18045}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18046}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18047}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
modeliza correctamente al concepto de función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-859-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18048}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18049}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18050}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable, entonces el concepto de conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-860-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18051}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18052}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18053}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-enumerable
recién definido modeliza correctamente al concepto de conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-861-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18054}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18055}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18056}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
enumerable. Nótese que según la definición que acabamos de escribir, un
conjunto no vacío
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-862-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18057}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18058}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18059}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18060}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18061}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18062}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18063}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18064}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18065}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18066}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18067}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18068}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18069}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18070}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18071}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18072}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\) es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-863-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18073}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18074}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18075}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-enumerable
si y solo si hay programas
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-864-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18076}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18077}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18078}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18079}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18080}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18081}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18082}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18083}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18084}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18085}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18086}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18087}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18088}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18089}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18090}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18091}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18092}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18093}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18094}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18095}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18096}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18097}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18098}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n + m}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n+m}\)
tales que

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  -
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-865-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18099}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18100}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18101}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18102}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18103}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18104}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18105}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18106}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18107}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18108}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18118}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18119}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18120}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18121}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18122}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18123}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18124}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18109}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18110}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18111}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18112}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18113}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18114}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18115}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18116}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18117}{}{{1}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18125}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18126}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18127}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18128}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18129}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18130}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18131}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18132}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18133}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18134}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18135}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18136}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18137}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18138}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18148}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18149}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18150}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18151}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18152}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18153}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18154}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18139}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18140}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18141}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18142}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18143}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18144}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18145}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18146}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18147}{}{{n}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18155}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18156}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18157}{}{{ω}}}}{\({Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{1}}^{1,0,\#}) = ... = {Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}}^{1,0,\#}) = \omega\)}}}\(\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{1}}^{1,0,\#})=...=\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}}^{1,0,\#})=\omega\)
\item
  -
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-866-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18158}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18159}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18160}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18161}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18162}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18163}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18164}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18165}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18166}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18167}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18179}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18180}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18181}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18182}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18183}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18184}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18185}{}{{∗}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18168}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18169}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18170}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18171}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18172}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18173}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18174}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18175}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18176}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18177}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18178}{}{{1}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18186}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18187}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18188}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18189}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18190}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18191}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18192}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18193}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18194}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18195}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18196}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18197}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18198}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18199}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18211}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18212}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18213}{}{{1}}\protect\hype + 1}}^{1,0, \ast}) = ... = {Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n} + m}^{1,0, \ast}) = \omega\)}}}\(\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+1}}^{1,0,\ast})=...=\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}+m}^{1,0,\ast})=\omega\)
\item
  -
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-867-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18221}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18222}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18223}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18224}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18225}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18226}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18227}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18228}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18229}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18230}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18231}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18241}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18242}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18243}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18244}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18245}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18246}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18247}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18232}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18233}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18234}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18235}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18236}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18237}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18238}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18239}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18240}{}{{1}}}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18248}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18249}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18250}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18251}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18252}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18253}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18254}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18264}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18265}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18266}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18267}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18268}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18269}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18270}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18255}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18256}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18257}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18258}{}{\protect\hyper = {Im}\lbrack\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{1}}^{1,0,\#},...,\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}}^{1,0,\#},\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n + 1}}^{1,0, \ast},...,\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n + m}}^{1,0, \ast}\rbrack\)}}}\(S=\mathrm{Im}[\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{1}}^{1,0,\#},...,\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}}^{1,0,\#},\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+1}}^{1,0,\ast},...,\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+m}}^{1,0,\ast}]\)
\end{enumerate}

Como puede notarse los programas
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-868-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18318}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18319}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18320}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18321}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18323}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18324}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18325}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18326}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18327}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18328}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18329}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18330}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18331}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18332}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18333}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18334}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18335}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18336}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18337}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18338}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18339}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18340}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n + m}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n+m}\)
puestos secuencialmente a funcionar desde el estado
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-869-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18341}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18342}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18343}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18344}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18345}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18346}{}{{∥}}}}}{\(\left\| x \right\|\)}}}\(\left\Vert x\right\Vert\)
producen en forma natural un
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3-procedimientos-efectivos.html\#definicion\%20de\%20procedimiento\%20efectivo}{procedimiento
efectivo} (con dato de entrada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-870-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18347}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18348}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18349}{}{{x}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18350}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18351}{}{{ω}}}}{\(x \in \omega\)}}}\(x\in\omega\))
que
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/3.3-conjuntos-sigma-efectivamente-enumerables.html\#definicion\%20de\%20procedimiento\%20efectivo\%20enumera\%20a\%20S}{enumera}
a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-871-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18352}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18353}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18354}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\).
Por supuesto podemos decir que en tal caso los programas
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-872-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18355}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18356}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18357}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18358}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18359}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18360}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18361}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18362}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18363}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18364}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18365}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18366}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18367}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18368}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18369}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18370}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18371}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18372}{}{{P}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18373}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18374}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18375}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18376}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18377}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n + m}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}_{1},...,\mathcal{P}_{n+m}\)
\emph{enumeran a}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-873-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18378}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18379}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18380}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\).
La siguiente proposición muestra que también las cosas se pueden hacer
con un solo programa

\leavevmode\vadjust pre{\hypertarget{Pux20enumeraux20aux20S}{}}%
\textbf{4.11} (Caracterización de
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-874-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18381}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18382}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18383}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-enumerabilidad).
\emph{Sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-875-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18384}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18385}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18386}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18387}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18388}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18389}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18390}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18391}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18392}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18393}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18394}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18395}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18396}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18397}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18398}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18399}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast m}\)
un conjunto no vacío. Entonces son equivalentes:

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  (1)
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-876-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18400}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18401}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-18402}{}\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}\[\begin{aligned}
F_{1} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{1}}^{1,0,\#}\\
F_{2} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{2}}^{1,0,\#}\\
& \vdots\\
F_{n} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n}}^{1,0,\#}\\
F_{n+1} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+1}}^{1,0,\ast}\\
F_{n+2} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+2}}^{1,0,\ast}\\
& \vdots\\
F_{n+m} & =\Psi_{\mathcal{P}_{n+m}}^{1,0,\ast}
\end{aligned}\] Nótese que cada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-922-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19727}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19728}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19729}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19730}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19731}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19732}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19733}{}{{i}}}}}}}}{\(F_{i}\)}}}\(F_{i}\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-923-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19734}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19735}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19736}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
y tiene dominio igual a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-924-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19737}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19738}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19739}{}{{ω}}}}{\(\omega\)}}}\(\omega\).
Sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-925-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19740}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19741}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19742}{}{{F}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19743}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19744}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19745}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19746}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19747}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19748}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19749}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19750}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19751}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19752}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19753}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19754}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19755}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19756}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19757}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19758}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19759}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19760}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19761}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19762}{}{{{]}}}}}{\(F = \lbrack F_{1},...,F_{n + m}\rbrack\)}}}\(F=[F_{1},...,F_{n+m}]\).
Tenemos por definición que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-926-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19763}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19764}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19765}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19766}{}{{D}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19767}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19768}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19769}{}{{F}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19770}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19771}{}{{ω}}}}{\(D_{F} = \omega\)}}}\(D_{F}=\omega\)
y ya que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-927-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19772}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19773}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19774}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19775}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19776}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19777}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19778}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19779}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19780}{}{{)}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19781}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19782}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19783}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19784}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19785}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19786}{}{{i}}}}}}}}{\(F_{(i)} = F_{i}\)}}}\(F_{(i)}=F_{i}\),
para cada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-928-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19787}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19788}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19789}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19790}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19791}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19792}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19793}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19794}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19795}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19796}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19797}{}{{n}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19798}{}{{+}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19799}{}{{m}}}}{\(i = 1,...,n + m\)}}}\(i=1,...,n+m\)
tenemos que cada
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-929-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19800}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19801}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19802}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19803}{}{{F}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19804}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19805}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19806}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19807}{}{{i}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19808}{}{{)}}}}}}}}{\(F_{(i)}\)}}}\(F_{(i)}\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-930-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19809}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19810}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19811}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable.
Dejamos al lector verificar que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-931-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19812}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19813}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19814}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19815}{}{{I}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19816}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19817}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19818}{}{{F}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19819}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19820}{}{{S}}}}{\(I_{F} = S\)}}}\(I_{F}=S\)
~

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20programaux20Pux20enumeraux20aux20S}{}{}Cuando
un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-932-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19821}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19822}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19823}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19824}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19825}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
cumpla las propiedades dadas en (3) de la proposición anterior respecto
de un conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-933-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19826}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19827}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19828}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\),
diremos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-934-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19829}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19830}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19831}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19832}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19833}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
\emph{enumera} a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-935-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19834}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19835}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19836}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\).
Nótese que:

\begin{enumerate}
\item
  - Si
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-936-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19837}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19838}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19839}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19840}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19841}{}{{ω}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega\)
  es no vacío, entonces
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-937-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19842}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19843}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19844}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19845}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19846}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
  enumera a
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-938-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19847}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19848}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19849}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\)
  sii
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-939-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19850}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19851}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19852}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19853}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19854}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19855}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19856}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19857}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19858}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19859}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19865}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19866}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19867}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19868}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19869}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19870}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19871}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19860}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19861}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19862}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19863}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19864}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19872}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19873}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19874}{}{{ω}}}}{\({Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,\#}) = \omega\)}}}\(\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,\#})=\omega\)
  y
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-940-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19875}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19876}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19877}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19878}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19879}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19880}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19881}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19882}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19883}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19889}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19890}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19891}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19892}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19893}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19894}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19895}{}{{\#}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19884}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19885}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19886}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19887}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19888}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19896}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19897}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19898}{}{{S}}}}{\({Im}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,\#}) = S\)}}}\(\mathrm{Im}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,\#})=S\)
\item
  - Si
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-941-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19899}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19900}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19901}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19902}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19903}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19904}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19905}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19906}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19907}{}{{∗}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \Sigma^{\ast}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\Sigma^{*}\)
  es no vacío, entonces
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-942-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19908}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19909}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19910}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19911}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19912}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
  enumera a
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-943-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19913}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19914}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19915}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\)
  sii
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-944-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19916}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19917}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19918}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19919}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19920}{}{{D}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19921}{}{{o}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19922}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19923}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19924}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19925}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19931}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19932}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19933}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19934}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19935}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19936}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19937}{}{{∗}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19926}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19927}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19928}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19929}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19930}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19938}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19939}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19940}{}{{ω}}}}{\({Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0, \ast}) = \omega\)}}}\(\mathrm{Dom}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,*})=\omega\)
  y
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-945-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19941}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19942}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19943}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19944}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19945}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19946}{}{{m}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19947}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19948}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19949}{}{{Ψ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19955}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19956}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19957}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19958}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19959}{}{{0}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19960}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19961}{}{{∗}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19950}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19951}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19952}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19953}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19954}{}{{P}}}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19962}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19963}{}{{=}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19964}{}{{S}}}}{\({Im}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0, \ast}) = S\)}}}\(\mathrm{Im}(\Psi_{\mathcal{P}}^{1,0,*})=S\)

Cabe destacar que
(3){{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-946-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19965}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19966}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19967}{}{{⇒}}}}{\(\Rightarrow\)}}}\(\Rightarrow\)(1)
de la proposición anterior es muy útil a la hora de probar que un
conjunto dado es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-947-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19968}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19969}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19970}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-enumerable
ya que nos permite trabajar dentro de un solo programa.

\hypertarget{conjuntos-sigma-computables}{%
\subsubsection[{4.3.6} Conjuntos
\(\Sigma\)-computables]{\texorpdfstring{{4.3.6}
\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20conjuntoux20sigma-computable}{}{}Conjuntos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-948-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19971}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19972}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19973}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computables}{4.3.6 Conjuntos Σ\textbackslash Sigma\textbackslash Sigma-computables}}\label{conjuntos-sigma-computables}}

La versión imperativa del concepto de conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-949-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19974}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19975}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19976}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-efectivamente
computable es fácil de dar: un conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-950-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19977}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19978}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19979}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19980}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19981}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19982}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19983}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19984}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19985}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19986}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19987}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19988}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19989}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19990}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19991}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19992}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast m}\)
será llamado
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-951-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19993}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19994}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19995}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)\emph{-computable}
cuando la función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-952-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19996}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19997}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19998}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-19999}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20003}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20004}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20005}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20006}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20007}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20008}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20009}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20010}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20011}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20012}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20013}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20014}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20015}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20016}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20000}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20001}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20002}{}{{S}}}}}}}}}{\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}\)}}}\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}}\) sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-953-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20017}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20018}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20019}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable.
O sea que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-954-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20020}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20021}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20022}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20023}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20024}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20025}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20026}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20027}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20028}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20029}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20030}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20031}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20032}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20033}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20034}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20035}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast m}\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-955-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20036}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20037}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20038}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
sii hay un programa
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-956-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20039}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20040}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20041}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20042}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20043}{}{{P}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20044}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20045}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20046}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20047}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20048}{}{{P}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20049}{}{{r}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20050}{}{{o}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20051}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20052}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20053}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P} \in {Pro}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\in\mathrm{Pro}^{\Sigma}\)
el cual computa a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-957-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20054}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20055}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20056}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20057}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20061}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20062}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20063}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20064}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20065}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20066}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20067}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20068}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20069}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20070}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20071}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20072}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20073}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20074}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20058}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20059}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20060}{}{{S}}}}}}}}}{\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}\)}}}\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast

\begin{enumerate}

  se detiene partiendo desde
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-960-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20097}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20098}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20099}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20100}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20101}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20102}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20103}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20104}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20105}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20106}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20107}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20108}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20109}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20110}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20111}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20112}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20113}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20114}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20115}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20116}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20117}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20118}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20119}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20120}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20121}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20122}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20123}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20124}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20125}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20126}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20127}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20128}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20129}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20130}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20131}{}{{∥}}}}}{\(\left\| x_{1},...x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \right\|\)}}}\(\left\Vert

  queda con contenido igual a

  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-964-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20173}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20174}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20175}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20176}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20177}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
  se detiene partiendo desde
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-965-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20178}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20179}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20180}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20181}{}{{∥}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20182}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20183}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20184}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20185}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20186}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20187}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20188}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20189}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20190}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20191}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20192}{}{{x}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20193}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20194}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20195}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20196}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20197}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20198}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20199}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20200}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20201}{}{{1}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20202}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20203}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20204}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20205}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20206}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20207}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20208}{}{{α}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20209}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20210}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20211}{}{{m}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20212}{}{{∥}}}}}{\(\left\| x_{1},...x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m} \right\|\)}}}\(\left\Vert
  x_{1},...x_{n},\alpha_{1},...,\alpha_{m}\right\Vert\) y la variable
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-966-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20213}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20214}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20215}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20216}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20217}{}{{N}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20218}{}{{1}}}}{\(N1\)}}}\(\mathrm{N}1\)
  queda con contenido igual a
  {{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-967-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20219}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20220}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20221}{}{{0}}}}{\(0\)}}}\(0\)
\end{enumerate}

\protect\hypertarget{definicionux20deux20programaux20Pux20decideux20laux20perteneciaux20aux20S}{}{}Si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-968-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20222}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20223}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20224}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20225}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20226}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
es un programa el cual computa a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-969-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20227}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20228}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20229}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20230}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20234}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20235}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20236}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20237}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20238}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20239}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20240}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20241}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20242}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20243}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20244}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20245}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20246}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20247}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20231}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20232}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20233}{}{{S}}}}}}}}}{\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}\)}}}\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}}\), diremos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-970-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20248}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20249}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20250}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20251}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20252}{}{{P}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{P}\)}}}\(\mathcal{P}\)
\emph{decide la pertenencia a}
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-971-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20253}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20254}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20255}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\),
con respecto al conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-972-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20256}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20257}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20258}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20259}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20260}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20261}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20262}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20263}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20264}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20265}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20266}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20267}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20268}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20269}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}\).

\hypertarget{macros-asociados-a-conjuntos-sigma-computables}{%
\paragraph*{\texorpdfstring{Macros asociados a conjuntos
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-973-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20270}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20271}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20272}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computables}{Macros asociados a conjuntos Σ\textbackslash Sigma\textbackslash Sigma-computables}}\label{macros-asociados-a-conjuntos-sigma-computables}}
\addcontentsline{toc}{paragraph}{Macros asociados a conjuntos
\(\Sigma\)-computables}

El Primer Manantial de Macros nos dice que si
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-974-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20273}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20274}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20275}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20276}{}{{⊆}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20277}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20278}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20279}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20280}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20281}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20282}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20283}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20284}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20285}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20286}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20287}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20288}{}{{m}}}}}}}}{\(S \subseteq \omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}\)}}}\(S\subseteq\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast m}\)
es un conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-975-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20289}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20290}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20291}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable,
entonces, ya que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-976-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20292}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20293}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20294}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20295}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20299}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20300}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20301}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20302}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20303}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20304}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20305}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20306}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20307}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20308}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20309}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20310}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20311}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20312}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20296}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20297}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20298}{}{{S}}}}}}}}}{\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}\)}}}\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}}\) es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-977-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20313}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20314}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20315}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable,
hay en
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-978-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20316}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20317}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20318}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20319}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20320}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20321}{}{{S}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20322}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20323}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20324}{}{{Σ}}}}}}}}{\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)}}}\(\mathcal{S}^{\Sigma}\)
un macro
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-979-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20325}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20326}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20327}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20328}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20329}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20330}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20331}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20332}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20333}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20334}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20335}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20339}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20340}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20341}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20342}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20343}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20344}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20345}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20346}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20347}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20348}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20349}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20350}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20351}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20352}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20336}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20337}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20338}{}{{S}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20353}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20354}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20355}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20356}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20357}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20358}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20359}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20360}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20361}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20362}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20363}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20364}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20365}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20366}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20367}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20368}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20370}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20369}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20371}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20372}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20373}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20374}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20375}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20376}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20377}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20378}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20379}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20380}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20381}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20382}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20383}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20384}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20385}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20386}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20388}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20387}{}{{m}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20389}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20390}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20391}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20392}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20393}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20394}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20395}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20396}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20397}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20398}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20399}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20400}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20401}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20402}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\[\left\lbrack {IF}\;\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}(V1,...,V\overline{n},W1,...,W\overline{m})\;{GOTO}\; A1 \right\rbrack\]}}}}\[\left[\mathrm{IF}\;\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}}(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\right]\]
Escribiremos el nombre de este macro de la siguiente manera mas
intuitiva:
{{}{\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-980-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20403}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20404}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20405}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20406}{}{{{[}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20407}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20408}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20409}{}{{I}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20410}{}{{F}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20411}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20412}{}{{(}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20413}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20414}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20415}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20416}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20417}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20418}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20419}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20420}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20421}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20422}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20423}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20424}{}{{V}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20425}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20426}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20427}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20429}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20428}{}{{n}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20430}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20431}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20432}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20433}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20434}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20435}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20436}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20437}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20438}{}{{.}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20439}{}{{,}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20440}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20441}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20442}{}{{W}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20443}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20444}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20445}{}{{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20447}{}{{¯}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20446}{}{{m}}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20448}{}{{)}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20449}{}{{∈}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20450}{}{{S}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20451}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20452}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20453}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20454}{}{{G}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20455}{}{{O}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20456}{}{{T}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20457}{}{{O}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20458}{}{}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20459}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20460}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20461}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20462}{}{{1}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20463}{}{{{]}}}}}}{\[\left\lbrack {IF}\;(V1,...,V\overline{n},W1,...,W\overline{m}) \in S\;{GOTO}\; A1 \right\rbrack\]}}}}\[\left[\mathrm{IF}\;(\mathrm{V}1,...,\mathrm{V}\bar{n},\mathrm{W}1,...,\mathrm{W}\bar{m})\in
S\;\mathrm{GOTO}\;\mathrm{A}1\right]\] Nótese que las expansiones de
este macro, dado que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-981-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20464}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20465}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20466}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20467}{}{{χ}}}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20471}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20472}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20473}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20474}{}{{ω}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20475}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20476}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20477}{}{{n}}}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20478}{}{{×}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20479}{}{{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20480}{}{{Σ}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20481}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20482}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20483}{}{{∗}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20484}{}{{m}}}}}}}}}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20468}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20469}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20470}{}{{S}}}}}}}}}{\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n} \times \Sigma^{\ast m}}\)}}}\(\chi_{S}^{\omega^{n}\times\Sigma^{\ast
m}}\) es
\href{https://granlogico.com/apunteweb/1.12-funciones-y-conjuntos-sigma-mixtos.html\#definicion\%20de\%20funcion\%20sigma-total}{{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-982-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20485}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20486}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20487}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}}\(\Sigma\)-total,
ya sea terminan por la última instrucción de la expansión o direccionan
a la primera instrucción que tenga label igual al label que reemplazo a
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-983-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20488}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20489}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20490}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20491}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20492}{}{{A}}}}\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20493}{}{{1}}}}{\(A1\)}}}\(\mathrm{A}1\)
en la expansión. Es importante notar que para asegurar la existencia de
este macro utilizamos que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-984-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20494}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20495}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20496}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\)
es
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-985-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20497}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20498}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20499}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
lo cual no siempre sucederá para un conjunto
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-986-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20500}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20501}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20502}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\).
Por ejemplo, puede pasar que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-987-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20503}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20504}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20505}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\)
sea el dominio de una función
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-988-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20506}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20507}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20508}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)\emph{-}computable
pero que
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-989-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20509}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20510}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20511}{}{{S}}}}{\(S\)}}}\(S\)
no sea
{{}\protect\hypertarget{MathJax-Element-990-Frame}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20512}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20513}{}{\protect\hypertarget{MJXc-Node-20514}{}{{Σ}}}}{\(\Sigma\)}}}\(\Sigma\)-computable
(esto se vera mas adelante) y en tal caso no existirá en
